VERSION=V1.5.2

[V1.0.0] 2025-08-10
奠基版本发布
- 核心工具集：发布了基础 Python 脚本工具包。
- 基础功能：支持 SKU 销量统计、库存上传以及基础交易数据的清洗与处理。

[V1.1.0] 2025-09-28
财务模块集成
- 多源数据集成：集成了 Order Earning 资金流数据源，实现了业财一体化。
- 逻辑优化：在交易处理逻辑中引入了基于哈希 (Hash) 的去重算法，提升了数据处理的准确性。
- 报表系统：发布了多维度的盈亏分析报表体系。

[V1.2.0] 2025-11-29
智能化运维模块
- 机器学习集成：集成了 K-Means 聚类和 PCA 降维算法，实现了 SKU 的自动化打标与分层。
- 高级分析工具：新增了 Listing 流量诊断工具与 Combo 组合策略评估模型。

[V1.3.0] 2025-12-02
Web 应用化转型
- UI/UX 全面升级：从命令行脚本迁移至 Streamlit Web 框架，实现了交互式可视化操作界面。
- CRM 客户管理模块：引入了基于 RFM (最近一次消费、消费频率、消费金额) 模型的客户价值分析功能，支持精准用户画像。

[V1.4.0] 2025-12-04
企业级架构重构
- 自动化 ETL 流水线：发布了覆盖数据加载 (Ingest)、解析 (Parsing)、转换 (Transformation) 和归档 (Archiving) 的全生命周期自动化处理流程。
- 灾难恢复系统：引入了具备时间点恢复能力的数据库备份与还原中心 (Backup & Restore Center)。
- 基础设施升级：实现了配置与代码的完全分离 (Configuration Decoupling)；前端架构全面迁移至组件化 UI 模式 (Component-Based UI)。

[V1.4.1] 2025-12-05
核心数据完整性与算法热修复
- ETL 智能去重 (Smart Upsert)：实施了基于时间窗口剪枝和四维复合主键 (Seller + Order + Item + Action) 匹配的分区去重策略，实现了毫秒级精准覆盖，彻底消除了误删历史数据的风险。
- 全链路归一化 (Global Normalization)：在所有分析器 (Sales, Profit, Ordering, Prediction) 中强制实施严格的 SKU 归一化标准（大写/去空格），解决了报表首列重复和统计偏差问题。
- 数据流加固 (Data Pipeline Hardening)：修复了 Repository 到 Analyzer 传输过程中的静默数据丢失问题；增强了数据仓库中日期格式解析的容错能力。
- Bug 修复：修正了销量统计分析中店铺分桶统计丢失的问题，并补全了智能补货计划中的状态备注字段。

[V1.5.0] 2025-12-05
企业级安全架构与性能革命
- 企业级安全架构 (Enterprise Security Architecture)：实施了 PBKDF2-SHA256 密码加密存储与防暴力破解策略；敏感操作引入“操作密码+确认短语”双重校验机制，全面提升系统安全性。
- 高性能 ETL 引擎 (High-Performance ETL Engine)：核心转换逻辑升级为 Pandas 向量化矩阵运算，摒弃低效循环，处理速度提升 20-50 倍；引入 Staging Table 原子写入策略，确保多店铺数据并发上传时的绝对一致性。
- 深度审计系统 (Deep Audit System)：发布了显微镜级业务审计日志，支持数据变更的“修改前 vs 修改后”逐字段比对，实现全链路操作可追溯。
- 用户权限与运维增强 (User Access & Ops Enhancement)：构建了基于 RBAC 的细粒度权限控制体系，支持针对 ETL、报表等模块的独立鉴权；新增数据库运维“危险区域”，支持一键重置测试环境（仅清空流水，保留用户与基础档案）。

[V1.5.1] 2025-12-07
全栈架构重构与在线报表中心
- 全栈架构治理 (Full-Stack Re-architecture)：完成了从脚本化向工程化的深度转型。确立了 UI/Service/Repository 三层架构边界，彻底解耦了 UI 层对数据库的直接依赖；标准化系统入口，并完成了根目录与工具脚本的深度清洗。
- 在线报表中心 (Online Report Center)：新增报表在线预览与管理功能。用户现在可以通过 APP 直接查看和管理所有生成的 BI 商业智能报表，实现了数据洞察的即时在线访问，无需下载 ZIP。
- 算法精度修正 (Algorithm Correction)：修复了报表生成引擎中的统计逻辑错误，优化了利润计算与成本分摊的精度，彻底解决了部分 SKU 统计偏差问题，确保了财务数据的准确性。
- 代码与安全标准化 (Code & Security Standardization)：统一了全站的基础设施逻辑（如 IP 获取与日志处理），消除了重复代码 (DRY)；将“操作密码+确认短语”的双重安全校验机制推广至库存与资料修改模块，填补了安全短板。

==================== START FILE: stop_server.sh ====================
#!/bin/bash
# stop_server.sh
# Update: 匹配 app.py

echo "🛑 正在停止 ERP 服务..."

# [Fix] grep "streamlit run app.py"
ERP_PID=$(ps aux | grep "streamlit run app.py" | grep -v grep | awk '{print $2}')

if [ -z "$ERP_PID" ]; then
    echo "⚠️  未找到正在运行的 Streamlit 服务 (app.py)。"
else
    for pid in $ERP_PID; do
        kill -9 $pid
        echo " 已终止 Streamlit 主进程 (PID: $pid)"
    done
fi

CAF_PID=$(ps aux | grep "caffeinate -s" | grep -v grep | awk '{print $2}')
if [ -z "$CAF_PID" ]; then
    echo "️  未找到相关的防休眠进程。"
else
    for pid in $CAF_PID; do
        kill $pid
        echo " 已终止防休眠进程 (PID: $pid)"
    done
fi

echo "================================================="
echo "🎉 所有服务已停止。"
==================== END FILE: stop_server.sh ====================


==================== START FILE: config.py ====================
import os
import re
from pathlib import Path
from dotenv import load_dotenv

# 加载 .env 文件
load_dotenv()


class Config:
    # =========================================================================
    # 1. 路径配置
    # =========================================================================
    BASE_DIR = Path(__file__).resolve().parent

    UPLOADER_DIR = BASE_DIR / "uploader"
    OUTPUT_DIR = BASE_DIR / "output"
    BACKUP_DIR = BASE_DIR / "backup"
    ASSETS_DIR = BASE_DIR / "assets"
    LOG_DIR = BASE_DIR / "logs"

    for _dir in [UPLOADER_DIR, OUTPUT_DIR, BACKUP_DIR, LOG_DIR]:
        _dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

    # =========================================================================
    # 2. 版本控制 (Version Control)
    # =========================================================================
    PATCH_NOTES_FILE = ASSETS_DIR / "patch_notes.txt"

    # 默认值
    APP_VERSION = "V1.0.0"
    VERSION_DATE = "Unknown Date"  # [New] 版本日期
    AUTHOR = "Aaron"  # [New] 作者署名
    PATCH_NOTES_LIST = []

    @classmethod
    def load_version_info(cls):
        """从 txt 文件加载版本号、日期和更新日志"""
        if not cls.PATCH_NOTES_FILE.exists():
            return

        try:
            with open(cls.PATCH_NOTES_FILE, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
                content = f.read().strip()

            # 按双换行符分割每个块
            blocks = content.split('\n\n')
            cls.PATCH_NOTES_LIST = []

            for block in blocks:
                block = block.strip()
                if not block: continue

                # 第一行提取版本号
                if block.startswith("VERSION="):
                    cls.APP_VERSION = block.split("=")[1].strip()
                    continue

                # 解析更新日志块
                # 格式: [V1.5.0] 2025-12-05 \n 描述内容
                lines = block.split('\n', 1)
                if len(lines) < 2: continue

                header = lines[0].strip()
                desc = lines[1].strip()

                # 正则提取: [V1.5.0] 2025-12-05
                match = re.match(r"\[(.*?)\]\s+(.*)", header)
                if match:
                    ver, date_str = match.groups()

                    # [New] 如果是当前版本，提取日期
                    if ver == cls.APP_VERSION:
                        cls.VERSION_DATE = date_str

                    cls.PATCH_NOTES_LIST.append({
                        "ver": ver,
                        "date": date_str,
                        "desc": desc
                    })
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"⚠️ Error loading patch notes: {e}")

    # =========================================================================
    # 3. 数据库配置
    # =========================================================================
    DB_HOST = os.getenv("DB_HOST", "localhost")
    DB_PORT = int(os.getenv("DB_PORT", 3306))
    DB_USER = os.getenv("DB_USER", "root")
    DB_PASS = os.getenv("DB_PASS", "")
    DB_NAME = os.getenv("DB_NAME", "MGMT")
    DB_CHARSET = os.getenv("DB_CHARSET", "utf8mb4")

    SQLALCHEMY_URL = (
        f"mysql+pymysql://{DB_USER}:{DB_PASS}@{DB_HOST}:{DB_PORT}/{DB_NAME}?charset={DB_CHARSET}"
    )

    # =========================================================================
    # 4. 安全配置
    # =========================================================================
    DB_OPERATOR_PWD = os.getenv("DB_OPERATOR_PWD", "1522")

    # =========================================================================
    # 5. 业务参数配置
    # =========================================================================
    LEAD_MONTH = 2.0
    MIN_SAFETY_MONTH = 1.0
    LOSS_RATES = {
        "CASE": 0.6, "REQUEST": 0.5, "RETURN": 0.3, "DISPUTE": 1.0
    }

    @classmethod
    def update_params(cls, lead_time=None, safety_month=None, loss_rates=None):
        if lead_time is not None: cls.LEAD_MONTH = lead_time
        if safety_month is not None: cls.MIN_SAFETY_MONTH = safety_month
        if loss_rates is not None: cls.LOSS_RATES.update(loss_rates)


# 模块加载时立即读取版本信息
Config.load_version_info()
==================== END FILE: config.py ====================

#!/bin/bash
# run_server.sh
# Eaglestar ERP 启动脚本
# Update: 指向 app.py

cd "$(dirname "$0")"
source .venv/bin/activate

nohup caffeinate -s > /dev/null 2>&1 &
CAFFEINATE_PID=$!

nohup streamlit run app.py > streamlit_output.log 2>&1 &
STREAMLIT_PID=$!

echo "================================================="
echo "🚀 ERP 已在后台启动 (PID: $STREAMLIT_PID)"
echo " 防休眠 PID: $CAFFEINATE_PID"
echo "Entry Point: app.py"
echo "================================================="
==================== END FILE: run_server.sh ====================

#!/bin/bash
# run_tests.sh
# 自动化测试执行脚本

echo "🧪 正在初始化测试环境..."
export PYTHONPATH=$PYTHONPATH:$(pwd)

# 检查 pytest 是否安装
if ! command -v pytest &> /dev/null; then
    echo " 未找到 pytest。正在尝试安装..."
    pip install pytest
fi

echo "🚀 开始运行单元测试..."
echo "---------------------------------------------------"

# 运行 pytest，-v 显示详细信息
pytest tests/test_core_units.py -v

EXIT_CODE=$?

echo "---------------------------------------------------"
if [ $EXIT_CODE -eq 0 ]; then
    echo " 所有测试通过！系统逻辑正常。"
else
    echo " 测试失败！请检查上述错误信息。"
fi

exit $EXIT_CODE

==================== START FILE: app.py ====================
# app.py
"""
Eaglestar ERP - Main Controller (Entry Point) V4.1
Standardized Entry Point.
"""
import time
import streamlit as st
from config import Config
from core.auth_service import AuthService
from core.context import set_current_user
from ui.main_interface import MainInterface
from ui.styles import StyleManager

# ==============================================================================
# 1. 全局配置 (必须是第一个 Streamlit 命令)
# ==============================================================================
st.set_page_config(
    page_title=f"Eaglestar ERP - {Config.APP_VERSION}",
    page_icon="🦅",
    layout="wide",
    initial_sidebar_state="collapsed",
)

# ==============================================================================
# 2. 系统初始化
# ==============================================================================
# 注入全局 CSS
StyleManager.apply_global_styles()

# 初始化核心服务
AuthService.initialize()

# 会话常量定义
SESSION_USER = "auth_user"
SESSION_LAST_ACTIVE = "last_active"
SESSION_TOKEN = "token"
AUTO_LOGOUT_SEC = 600  # 10分钟


def check_session_security() -> str:
    """
    [中间件] 会话安全检查
    返回: 踢出原因 (kickout_msg)，如果为 None 则表示会话正常
    """
    if SESSION_USER not in st.session_state:
        return None

    user_data = st.session_state[SESSION_USER]
    username = user_data.get("username")

    # 1. 设置上下文 (Context)
    set_current_user(username, ip=user_data.get("ip"))

    # 2. 活跃度续期 (Heartbeat)
    st.session_state[SESSION_LAST_ACTIVE] = time.time()

    # 3. 单点登录互斥检查 (SSO Check)
    local_token = st.session_state.get(SESSION_TOKEN)
    if not AuthService.verify_session_token(username, local_token):
        return "⚠️ 您已在其他设备登录，当前会话已失效 (被迫下线)。"

    # 4. 超时自动注销检查 (Timeout Check) - 逻辑预留
    return None


def main():
    """主程序入口"""

    # --- Phase 1: 安全检查 ---
    kickout_msg = check_session_security()

    if kickout_msg:
        st.session_state.clear()
        # 强制跳转回登录页并显示错误
        MainInterface.render_login_page(SESSION_USER, SESSION_LAST_ACTIVE, SESSION_TOKEN, kickout_msg)
        return

    # --- Phase 2: 路由分发 ---
    if SESSION_USER not in st.session_state:
        # 未登录 -> 渲染登录页
        MainInterface.render_login_page(SESSION_USER, SESSION_LAST_ACTIVE, SESSION_TOKEN)
    else:
        # 已登录 -> 渲染主应用
        try:
            user_data = st.session_state[SESSION_USER]
            MainInterface.render_main_app(user_data, SESSION_USER)
        except Exception as e:
            st.error(f"Critical UI Error: {e}")
            if st.button("Emergency Reset"):
                st.session_state.clear()
                st.rerun()


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
==================== END FILE: app.py ====================


==================== START FILE: ui/layout.py ====================
# ui/layout.py

import streamlit as st
import base64
import streamlit.components.v1 as components
from config import Config


# ==============================================================================
# 资源加载辅助函数
# ==============================================================================
def get_base64_encoded_file(file_path):
    """读取文件并转换为 base64 编码"""
    try:
        with open(file_path, "rb") as f:
            return base64.b64encode(f.read()).decode("utf-8")
    except FileNotFoundError:
        return None


# ==============================================================================
# 1. 背景动画渲染 (暴力穿透版)
# ==============================================================================
def set_main_background_video():
    """
    渲染全屏背景视频，强制覆盖 Streamlit 默认背景
    """
    video_path = Config.ASSETS_DIR / "background.mp4"
    video_b64 = get_base64_encoded_file(video_path)

    if not video_b64:
        return

    # 核心 CSS：暴力将所有可能遮挡视频的容器设为透明
    css_code = f"""
    <style>
        /* 1. 全局容器透明化 */
        .stApp {{
            background: transparent !important;
        }}
        /* 2. 滚动容器透明化 */
        [data-testid="stAppViewContainer"] {{
            background: transparent !important;
        }}
        /* 3. 主内容区透明化 */
        [data-testid="stMainBlockContainer"] {{
            background: transparent !important;
        }}
        /* 4. 顶部 Header 透明化 */
        [data-testid="stHeader"] {{
            background: transparent !important;
            visibility: hidden; /* 彻底隐藏默认菜单栏 */
        }}

        /* 5. 背景视频定位 */
        #bg-video {{
            position: fixed;
            top: 0;
            left: 0;
            width: 100vw;
            height: 100vh;
            object-fit: cover;
            z-index: -100;
        }}

        /* 6. 黑色遮罩 */
        #bg-overlay {{
            position: fixed;
            top: 0;
            left: 0;
            width: 100vw;
            height: 100vh;
            background: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.70);
            z-index: -99;
            backdrop-filter: blur(3px);
        }}

        /* 7. 侧边栏样式 */
        [data-testid="stSidebar"] {{
            background-color: rgba(20, 20, 20, 0.9) !important;
            border-right: 1px solid rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1);
            backdrop-filter: blur(10px);
        }}

        /* 8. 全局字体增强 */
        h1, h2, h3, h4, h5, h6, p, span, div, label, li {{
            color: #E0E0E0 !important;
            text-shadow: 0px 1px 2px rgba(0,0,0,0.8);
        }}

        /* 9. 输入框组件美化 */
        .stTextInput input, .stNumberInput input, .stDateInput input, .stSelectbox div[data-baseweb="select"] {{
            background-color: rgba(40, 40, 40, 0.6) !important;
            color: white !important;
            border: 1px solid rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.2) !important;
        }}
    </style>
    """

    video_html = f"""
    {css_code}
    <video id="bg-video" autoplay loop muted playsinline>
        <source src="data:video/mp4;base64,{video_b64}" type="video/mp4">
    </video>
    <div id="bg-overlay"></div>
    """
    st.markdown(video_html, unsafe_allow_html=True)


# ==============================================================================
# 2. 头部渲染 (Logo + 时钟 + 动态版本号 + 作者信息)
# ==============================================================================

    """

    """

        f'<img src="data:image/png;base64,{logo_b64}" class="header-logo">'
        if logo_b64 else "🦅"

        <style>

            display: flex;

            border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.15);

        </style>

        <div class="header-wrapper">
            <div class="header-left">
                {logo_img}
                <div>
                    <div class="main-title">Eaglestar ERP</div>
                    <div class="sub-title">Enterprise Intelligence Platform {Config.APP_VERSION}</div>

                </div>
            </div>
            <div class="header-right">
                <span class="company-badge">🦅 EAGLESTAR INC.</span>
                <div id="clock-display">Initializing...</div>
            </div>
        </div>
    """, unsafe_allow_html=True)

    # JS 时钟
    js_code = """
    <script>
        function updateClock() {
            const now = new Date();
            const dateStr = now.getFullYear() + "-" + 
                            String(now.getMonth()+1).padStart(2, '0') + "-" + 
                            String(now.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
            const timeStr = String(now.getHours()).padStart(2, '0') + ":" + 
                            String(now.getMinutes()).padStart(2, '0') + ":" + 
                            String(now.getSeconds()).padStart(2, '0');
            try {
                const clock = window.parent.document.getElementById('clock-display');
                if (clock) {
                    clock.innerText = "🕒 " + dateStr + " " + timeStr;
                }
            } catch(e) {
                console.log("Clock element not found");
            }
        }
        setInterval(updateClock, 1000);
        updateClock();
    </script>
    """
    components.html(js_code, height=0)
==================== END FILE: ui/layout.py ====================

# ui/main_interface.py

import streamlit as st
import time
import requests
import datetime
from config import Config
from core.auth_service import AuthService
from core.context import set_current_user, clear_context
from ui.layout import set_main_background_video, render_header, get_base64_encoded_file

# 引入所有页面 (新增 data_visualization)
from ui.pages import (
    home, etl_ingest, reports, db_data_change, db_admin, user_admin, audit_logs, ai_gemini,
    data_visualization  # [New]
)


class MainInterface:
    """
    负责处理登录页和主界面的渲染逻辑
    V3.4 Upgrade: 新增数据可视化模块入口
    """

    # =========================================================================
    # 1. 智能感知模块
    # =========================================================================

    @staticmethod
    def get_client_ip() -> str:
        """获取客户端真实 IP (官方标准版)"""
        try:
            # [Fix] 使用官方 st.context.headers 替代旧 Hack
            headers = st.context.headers
            if headers:
                # Cloudflare 传递的真实 IP
                if "Cf-Connecting-Ip" in headers:
                    return headers["Cf-Connecting-Ip"]
                # 标准代理头
                if "X-Forwarded-For" in headers:
                    return headers["X-Forwarded-For"].split(",")[0].strip()

            # 本地兜底
            session_info = st.runtime.get_instance().get_client_session_info()
            if hasattr(session_info, 'ip'): return session_info.ip
        except:
            pass
        return "UNKNOWN"

    @staticmethod
    @st.cache_data(ttl=3600)
    def get_smart_info(ip: str):
        info = {
            "city": "Unknown City", "weather_icon": "🌤️", "weather_desc": "Weather n/a",
            "temp": "--", "greeting": "Hello", "tips": "Welcome back!"
        }

        if ip in ["UNKNOWN", "127.0.0.1", "localhost", "::1"]:
            info["city"] = "Localhost"
            return info

        try:
            loc_url = f"http://ip-api.com/json/{ip}"
            loc_res = requests.get(loc_url, timeout=3).json()

            if loc_res.get("status") == "success":
                lat, lon = loc_res["lat"], loc_res["lon"]
                info["city"] = loc_res.get("city", "Unknown")
                timezone = loc_res.get("timezone", "UTC")

                weather_url = f"https://api.open-meteo.com/v1/forecast?latitude={lat}&longitude={lon}&current_weather=true&timezone={timezone}"
                w_res = requests.get(weather_url, timeout=3).json()

                if "current_weather" in w_res:
                    curr = w_res["current_weather"]
                    temp = curr["temperature"]
                    code = curr["weathercode"]
                    is_day = curr["is_day"]

                    info["temp"] = f"{temp}°C"

                    if code == 0:
                        info["weather_desc"] = "晴朗";
                        info["weather_icon"] = "☀️" if is_day else "🌙"
                    elif code in [1, 2, 3]:
                        info["weather_desc"] = "多云";
                        info["weather_icon"] = "⛅"
                    elif code in [45, 48]:
                        info["weather_desc"] = "有雾";
                        info["weather_icon"] = "🌫️"
                    elif 51 <= code <= 67:
                        info["weather_desc"] = "有雨";
                        info["weather_icon"] = "🌧️"
                    elif 71 <= code <= 77:
                        info["weather_desc"] = "下雪";
                        info["weather_icon"] = "❄️"
                    elif code >= 95:
                        info["weather_desc"] = "雷暴";
                        info["weather_icon"] = "⛈️"

                    try:
                        import pytz
                        local_tz = pytz.timezone(timezone)
                        local_hour = datetime.datetime.now(local_tz).hour
                    except:
                        local_hour = datetime.datetime.now().hour

                    if 5 <= local_hour < 12:
                        info["greeting"] = "早上好"
                    elif 12 <= local_hour < 14:
                        info["greeting"] = "中午好"
                    elif 14 <= local_hour < 19:
                        info["greeting"] = "下午好"
                    elif 19 <= local_hour < 23:
                        info["greeting"] = "晚上好"
                    else:
                        info["greeting"] = "夜深了"

                    tips = []
                    if local_hour >= 23 or local_hour < 5:
                        tips.append("工作虽重要，但也请注意休息哦 🌙")
                    elif 12 <= local_hour < 14:
                        tips.append("记得按时吃饭，小憩一下精力更充沛 ☕")
                    if "雨" in info["weather_desc"] or "雷" in info["weather_desc"]:
                        tips.append("外面下雨了，出行记得带伞 ☂️")
                    elif temp < 10:
                        tips.append("气温较低，注意保暖 🧣")
                    elif temp > 30:
                        tips.append("天气炎热，注意防暑降温 🥤")
                    if not tips: tips.append("愿你今天拥有好心情 ")
                    info["tips"] = tips[0]
        except Exception:
            pass
        return info

    # 2. 登录页渲染

    @staticmethod
    def render_login_page(session_key, last_active_key, token_key, msg_override=None):
        set_main_background_video()
        clear_context()
        _, col_center, _ = st.columns([1, 1.5, 1])

        with col_center:
            logo_path = Config.ASSETS_DIR / "Logo.png"
            logo_b64 = get_base64_encoded_file(logo_path)
            if logo_b64:
                logo_html = f'<img src="data:image/png;base64,{logo_b64}" style="width: 700px;max-width: 100%; height: auto; margin-bottom: 30px;">'
            else:
                logo_html = '<div style="font-size: 320px;line-height: 1.1; margin-bottom: 20px;">🦅</div>'

            st.markdown(
                f'<div style="margin-top: 60px; padding: 50px 30px; background: rgba(18, 18, 28, 0.95); border-radius: 20px; border: 1px solid rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); box-shadow: 0 25px 60px rgba(0,0,0,0.9); text-align: center; backdrop-filter: blur(12px);">{logo_html}<div style="font-size: 32px; font-weight: 800; color: #FFFFFF; letter-spacing: 2px; text-transform: uppercase;">Eaglestar ERP</div><div style="font-size: 15px; color: #4EC9B0; margin-top: 10px; font-family: \'Courier New\', monospace; font-weight: bold;">Enterprise Edition {Config.APP_VERSION}</div><div style="margin-top: 40px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.15);"></div></div>',
                unsafe_allow_html=True)

            if msg_override: st.warning(msg_override)
            st.markdown("###")
            with st.form("login_form"):
                u = st.text_input("用户名", placeholder="请输入账号")
                p = st.text_input("密码", type="password", placeholder="请输入密码")
                st.caption("🔒 安全提示：连续输错 10 次密码将自动锁定账号。")
                if st.form_submit_button("登录系统 (Sign In)", type="primary", use_container_width=True):
                    with st.spinner("正在验证身份..."):
                        # [Fix] 调用更新后的 get_client_ip
                        ip = MainInterface.get_client_ip()
                        ok, user, msg = AuthService.authenticate(u, p, ip=ip)
                        time.sleep(0.5)

                    if ok and user:
                        token = AuthService.refresh_session_token(user.username)
                        st.session_state[session_key] = {"username": user.username, "is_admin": user.is_admin, "ip": ip}
                        st.session_state[last_active_key] = time.time()
                        st.session_state[token_key] = token

                        set_current_user(user.username, ip=ip)
                        AuthService.record_login_event(user.username, ip)
                        st.success(f" 登录成功 (IP: {ip})")
                        time.sleep(0.5)
                        st.rerun()
                    else:
                        st.error(f" {msg}")

                    <div>🌐 <b>IP:</b> {ip}</div>
                </div>
            </div>
            """
            st.markdown(card_html, unsafe_allow_html=True)

            if st.button("🚪 退出登录", use_container_width=True):
                st.session_state.clear()
                st.rerun()

            st.markdown("###")
            st.markdown("#### ≡ 导航菜单")

            # [Mod] 新增 Visuals 模块
            menu_items = [
                ("🏠 系统首页 (Home)", "home"),
                ("🤖 Google Gemini (AI)", "gemini"),
                ("🔌 上传数据 (ETL)", "etl"),
                ("📊 商业智能报表 (BI)", "reports")
            ]

            # 仅管理员可见
            if is_admin:
                menu_items.append(("📈 数据交互可视化 (Visuals)", "visuals"))

            menu_items.extend([
                ("🛠️ 修改数据库 (Data)", "db_modify"),
                ("🗄️ 数据库运维 (DB Ops)", "db_admin")
            ])

            if is_admin:
                menu_items.extend([("👤 用户管理 (Admin)", "user_admin"), ("📜 审计日志 (Audit)", "audit_logs")])

            sel = st.radio("Go to", [m[0] for m in menu_items], label_visibility="collapsed")
            sel_key = next(item[1] for item in menu_items if item[0] == sel)

        with col_content:
            if not MainInterface._check_access(username, is_admin, sel_key):
                st.error(" 权限不足 (Access Denied)");
                st.info("请联系管理员开通权限。")
            else:
                if sel_key == "home":
                    home.render()
                elif sel_key == "gemini":
                    ai_gemini.render()
                elif sel_key == "etl":
                    etl_ingest.render()
                elif sel_key == "reports":
                    reports.render()
                # [Mod] 新增路由分支
                elif sel_key == "visuals":
                    data_visualization.render()
                elif sel_key == "db_modify":
                    db_data_change.render()
                elif sel_key == "db_admin":
                    db_admin.render()
                elif sel_key == "user_admin":
                    user_admin.render()
                elif sel_key == "audit_logs":
                    audit_logs.render()

    @staticmethod
    def _check_access(username, is_admin, module_key):
        # 基础公共模块
        if module_key in ["home", "reports", "gemini"]: return True

        # [New] 可视化模块仅限管理员
        if module_key == "visuals":
            return is_admin

        # 管理员拥有所有权限
        if is_admin: return True

        # 普通用户权限表检查
        key_map = {
            "etl": "module.etl",
            "db_modify": "module.db_modify",
            "db_admin": "module.db_admin",
            "user_admin": "module.user_admin",
            "audit_logs": "module.audit_logs"
        }
        db_key = key_map.get(module_key)
        if not db_key: return False
        return AuthService.get_permissions(username).get(db_key, False)

# ui/utils.py

import sys
import time
import datetime
import re
import html
import io
import csv
import importlib
from pathlib import Path
from typing import List, Tuple, Optional
from contextlib import contextmanager
import pandas as pd
import streamlit as st
import tqdm

# 引入配置以获取项目根目录
from config import Config

# ==============================================================================
# [Critical Fix] 健壮性加固
# ==============================================================================
if hasattr(tqdm, 'tqdm') and not isinstance(tqdm.tqdm, type):
    importlib.reload(tqdm)


# ==============================================================================
# 1. 通用工具函数 (Common Utilities)
# ==============================================================================
def get_client_ip() -> str:
    """
    [标准版] 获取客户端真实 IP
    优先从请求头获取 (Cloudflare/Proxy)，兜底使用 Session Info。
    """
    try:
        # 1. 尝试从 Streamlit 官方 Headers 获取 (1.30+)
        headers = st.context.headers
        if headers:
            # Cloudflare
            if "Cf-Connecting-Ip" in headers:
                return headers["Cf-Connecting-Ip"]
            # Standard Proxy
            if "X-Forwarded-For" in headers:
                return headers["X-Forwarded-For"].split(",")[0].strip()

        # 2. 尝试从底层 Session 获取 (Hack for local/older versions)
        session_info = st.runtime.get_instance().get_client_session_info()
        if hasattr(session_info, 'ip'):
            return session_info.ip

    except Exception:
        pass

    return "UNKNOWN"


def parse_compound_csv(file_path: Path) -> List[Tuple[str, pd.DataFrame]]:
    """
    [智能解析器] 解析包含多个子表的复杂 CSV 文件 (修复 Expected X fields saw Y 错误)

    原理：
    1. 按行读取文件。
    2. 识别分隔符（空行或标题行）。
    3. 将连续的数据块切割并独立转为 DataFrame。

    Returns:
        List of (Title, DataFrame)
    """
    if not file_path.exists():
        return []

    tables = []
    current_lines = []
    current_title = "Main Table"

    # 关键词识别标题行 (Profit表用 ===, Shipping表用 表X, 英文用 Table)
    title_pattern = re.compile(r'^(===.+===|表\d+|Table\s*\d+)', re.IGNORECASE)

    try:
        with open(file_path, "r", encoding="utf-8-sig") as f:
            all_lines = f.readlines()

        for line in all_lines:
            stripped = line.strip()

            # Case 1: 空行 -> 可能是分隔符
            if not stripped:
                if current_lines:
                    # 尝试将缓冲区解析为表
                    try:
                        # 过滤掉纯注释行
                        valid_lines = [l for l in current_lines if not l.startswith("#")]
                        if valid_lines:
                            csv_io = io.StringIO("".join(valid_lines))
                            df = pd.read_csv(csv_io)
                            if not df.empty and len(df.columns) > 1:
                                tables.append((current_title, df))
                    except:
                        pass
                    current_lines = []
                continue

            # Case 2: 标题行 -> 强制分隔
            # 如果行里没有逗号，且符合标题特征
            if "," not in stripped and title_pattern.match(stripped):
                # 先保存之前的 buffer
                if current_lines:
                    try:
                        csv_io = io.StringIO("".join(current_lines))
                        df = pd.read_csv(csv_io)
                        if not df.empty and len(df.columns) > 1:
                            tables.append((current_title, df))
                    except:
                        pass
                    current_lines = []

                # 更新标题 (去掉 ===)
                current_title = stripped.replace("===", "").strip()
                continue

            # Case 3: 报表底部的说明文字 (Footer)
            # 特征：很长，或者以 "说明"、"备注" 开头，且逗号很少
            if (stripped.startswith("说明") or stripped.startswith(
                    "备注") or "逻辑说明" in stripped) and stripped.count(',') < 2:
                # 遇到 Footer，直接结束当前的收集
                if current_lines:
                    try:
                        csv_io = io.StringIO("".join(current_lines))
                        df = pd.read_csv(csv_io)
                        if not df.empty:
                            tables.append((current_title, df))
                    except:
                        pass
                    current_lines = []
                # Footer 不作为 DataFrame 展示
                continue

            # Case 4: 普通数据行
            current_lines.append(line)

        # Loop 结束，处理最后一块
        if current_lines:
            try:
                csv_io = io.StringIO("".join(current_lines))
                df = pd.read_csv(csv_io)
                if not df.empty:
                    tables.append((current_title, df))
            except:
                pass

    except Exception as e:
        print(f"解析 CSV 失败: {e}")
        # 兜底：尝试作为单表读取
        try:
            df = pd.read_csv(file_path)
            return [("Raw Data", df)]
        except:
            return []

    return tables


# ==============================================================================
# 2. 日志处理器 (Log Handlers)
# ==============================================================================
class StreamlitLogHandler:
    """
    [UI组件] 双流日志处理器 (Dual-Stream Log Handler)
    """

    def __init__(self, container, original_stdout, max_height_css="240px"):
        self.container = container
        self.original_stdout = original_stdout  # 保存原始控制台管道
        self.buffer = []
        self.base_dir_str = str(Config.BASE_DIR).replace("\\", "/")

        self.css_style = f"""
            <style>
            .log-box {{
                height: {max_height_css};
                overflow-y: auto;
                background-color: #1e1e1e;
                color: #e0e0e0;
                padding: 12px;
                border-radius: 6px;
                font-family: 'Menlo', 'Consolas', monospace;
                font-size: 13px;
                border: 1px solid #444;
                white-space: pre-wrap;
                word-wrap: break-word;
                line-height: 1.5;
                display: flex;
                flex-direction: column;
            }}
            .log-meta {{ color: #808080; font-size: 0.85em; margin-right: 8px; }}
            .log-success {{ color: #4ec9b0; font-weight: bold; }}
            .log-error {{ color: #f44336; font-weight: bold; }}
            .log-warn {{ color: #cca700; }}
            </style>
        """

    def _sanitize_for_ui(self, text: str) -> str:
        clean_text = text.replace("\\", "/")
        if self.base_dir_str in clean_text:
            clean_text = clean_text.replace(self.base_dir_str, ".")
        clean_text = re.sub(r'/(?:Users|home)/[^/]+', '~', clean_text)

        css_class = ""
        if "" in clean_text or "成功" in clean_text:
            css_class = "log-success"
        elif "" in clean_text or "失败" in clean_text or "Error" in clean_text:
            css_class = "log-error"
        elif "⚠️" in clean_text or "Warning" in clean_text:
            css_class = "log-warn"

        escaped = html.escape(clean_text)
        if css_class:
            return f'<span class="{css_class}">{escaped}</span>'
        else:
            return escaped

    def write(self, text):
        self.original_stdout.write(text)
        if not text or text == "\n" or text == "\r": return

        timestamp = datetime.datetime.now().strftime("%H:%M:%S")
        sanitized_msg = self._sanitize_for_ui(text.strip())
        line_html = f'<div><span class="log-meta">[{timestamp}]</span>{sanitized_msg}</div>'
        self.buffer.append(line_html)

        if len(self.buffer) > 80:
            self.buffer.pop(0)

        content = "".join(self.buffer)
        js_scroll = """
        <script>
            try {
                var box = window.parent.document.getElementById("log-container-div");
                if (!box) box = document.getElementById("log-container-div");
                if (box) box.scrollTop = box.scrollHeight;
            } catch(e) {}
        </script>
        """
        full_html = f'{self.css_style}<div id="log-container-div" class="log-box">{content}</div>{js_scroll}'
        self.container.markdown(full_html, unsafe_allow_html=True)

    def flush(self):
        self.original_stdout.flush()


class StreamlitTqdm(tqdm.tqdm):
    def __init__(self, iterable=None, desc=None, total=None, leave=True, file=None,
                 cols=100, mininterval=0.1, maxinterval=10.0, miniters=None,
                 ascii=None, disable=False, unit='it', unit_scale=False,
                 dynamic_ncols=False, smoothing=0.3, bar_format=None, initial=0,
                 position=None, postfix=None, unit_divisor=1000, write_bytes=False,
                 lock_args=None, nrows=None, colour=None, delay=0, gui=False,
                 **kwargs):
        self.st_progress_bar = kwargs.pop('st_progress_bar', None)
        self.st_status_text = kwargs.pop('st_status_text', None)
        super().__init__(iterable, desc, total, leave, file, cols, mininterval,
                         maxinterval, miniters, ascii, disable, unit, unit_scale,
                         dynamic_ncols, smoothing, bar_format, initial, position,
                         postfix, unit_divisor, write_bytes, lock_args, nrows,
                         colour, delay, gui, **kwargs)

    def display(self, msg=None, pos=None):
        if self.total and self.total > 0:
            pct = max(0, min(1.0, self.n / self.total))
        else:
            pct = 0.0
        if self.st_progress_bar:
            self.st_progress_bar.progress(pct)
        if self.st_status_text:
            elapsed_str = self.format_interval(self.format_dict['elapsed'])
            status_msg = f"🔄 **{self.desc or 'Processing'}** | {int(pct * 100)}% | ⏳ {elapsed_str}"
            self.st_status_text.markdown(status_msg)
        return True


@contextmanager
def task_monitor(title: str = "任务执行中"):
    st.markdown(f"### {title}")
    c1, c2 = st.columns([1, 5])
    c1.markdown("**总体进度**")
    main_bar = c2.progress(0)
    c3, c4 = st.columns([1, 5])
    c3.markdown("**当前任务**")
    sub_bar = c4.progress(0)
    status_text = st.empty()
    log_container = st.empty()

    original_stdout = sys.stdout
    original_tqdm = tqdm.tqdm
    logger = StreamlitLogHandler(log_container, original_stdout)
    sys.stdout = logger

    def custom_tqdm_factory(*args, **kwargs):
        kwargs['st_progress_bar'] = sub_bar
        kwargs['st_status_text'] = status_text
        return StreamlitTqdm(*args, **kwargs)

    tqdm.tqdm = custom_tqdm_factory

    class MonitorController:
        def update_main_progress(self, percent: float):
            main_bar.progress(max(0.0, min(1.0, percent)))

        def log(self, msg: str):
            print(msg)

    try:
        yield MonitorController()
    finally:
        sys.stdout = original_stdout
        tqdm.tqdm = original_tqdm
        status_text.empty()
==================== END FILE: ui/utils.py ====================


==================== START FILE: ui/styles.py ====================
# ui/styles.py
import streamlit as st

class StyleManager:
    """
    [UI组件] 全局样式管理器

    """

    # 核心组件样式 (Tab, Radio, 等)
    _MAIN_STYLES = """

        /* 隐藏默认组件 */

    @classmethod
    def apply_global_styles(cls):
        """注入全局 CSS"""

# ui/components/inventory_wizard.py

import streamlit as st
import time
from datetime import date
from config import Config
from core.etl.inventory import InventoryLoader
from core.services.correction_service import CorrectionService
from core.services.file_service import FileService


class InventoryWizard:
    """
    [UI组件] 库存同步向导 (Inventory Wizard) - Enterprise V2.0

    职责:
    1. 上传库存 CSV。
    2. 校验 SKU 合法性 (与 Data_COGS 比对)。
    3. 提供非法 SKU 的修复/新增入口。
    4. 执行最终入库同步。
    """

    def __init__(self):
        self.loader = InventoryLoader()
        self.corrector = CorrectionService()  # 用于模糊搜索建议
        self.fs = FileService()
        self._init_state()

    def _init_state(self):
        if 'inv_state' not in st.session_state:
            st.session_state.inv_state = 'UPLOAD'
        if 'inv_df' not in st.session_state:
            st.session_state.inv_df = None
        if 'inv_errors' not in st.session_state:
            st.session_state.inv_errors = []
        if 'inv_error_idx' not in st.session_state:
            st.session_state.inv_error_idx = 0

    def _reset(self):
        for k in ['inv_state', 'inv_df', 'inv_errors', 'inv_error_idx', 'inv_target_month', 'inv_file_path']:
            if k in st.session_state: del st.session_state[k]
        st.rerun()

    def render(self):
        state = st.session_state.inv_state
        if state == 'UPLOAD':
            self._step_upload()
        elif state == 'FIXING':
            self._step_fixing()
        elif state == 'COMMIT':
            self._step_commit()

    # --- Step 1: Upload ---
    def _step_upload(self):
        st.info("步骤 1: 上传库存盘点文件 (需包含 SKU, Quantity 列)")

        c1, c2 = st.columns([2, 1])
        with c1:
            inv_file = st.file_uploader("选择 CSV 文件", type=['csv'], key="inv_up")
        with c2:
            default_date = date.today().replace(day=1)
            target_date = st.date_input("归属月份", value=default_date)
            # 格式化为 YYYY-MM
            target_month = target_date.strftime("%Y-%m")

        if st.button("🔍 开始校验", type="primary", use_container_width=True):
            if not inv_file:
                st.error("请先上传文件")
                return

            # 保存临时文件
            temp_path = Config.UPLOADER_DIR / inv_file.name
            Config.UPLOADER_DIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
            with open(temp_path, "wb") as f:
                f.write(inv_file.getbuffer())

            # 调用 Service 校验
            with st.spinner("正在校验 SKU..."):
                passed, unknown_skus, df_clean = self.loader.validate_file(temp_path)

            # 更新状态
            st.session_state.inv_df = df_clean
            st.session_state.inv_target_month = target_month
            st.session_state.inv_file_path = temp_path

            if passed:
                st.session_state.inv_state = 'COMMIT'
                st.success(" 校验通过！")
                time.sleep(0.5)
                st.rerun()
            else:
                st.session_state.inv_errors = sorted(unknown_skus)
                st.session_state.inv_error_idx = 0
                st.session_state.inv_state = 'FIXING'
                st.warning(f"⚠️ 发现 {len(unknown_skus)} 个未知 SKU，进入修复向导。")
                time.sleep(1)
                st.rerun()

    # --- Step 2: Fix ---
    def _step_fixing(self):
        errors = st.session_state.inv_errors
        idx = st.session_state.inv_error_idx
        total = len(errors)

        if idx >= total:
            st.session_state.inv_state = 'COMMIT'
            st.rerun()
            return

        bad_sku = errors[idx]
        pct = (idx + 1) / total
        st.progress(pct, text=f"修复进度: {idx + 1}/{total}")

        c_left, c_right = st.columns([1, 2])

        with c_left:
            st.error(f" 未知 SKU: **{bad_sku}**")
            # 统计该 SKU 在文件中的总数
            df = st.session_state.inv_df
            qty = df[df['SKU'] == bad_sku]['Quantity'].sum()
            st.caption(f"文件内总数量: {qty}")

        with c_right:
            tab_map, tab_new = st.tabs(["🔗 映射到现有 SKU", "➕ 注册为新 SKU"])

            # Option A: Map
            with tab_map:
                suggestions = self.corrector.get_fuzzy_suggestions(bad_sku)
                # 使用 selectbox 支持搜索
                # 既然是 Service，我们应该从 corrector 获取所有 valid_skus，但这里为了性能，
                # 我们假设 valid_skus 已经在 corrector.valid_skus 中缓存
                all_valid = sorted(list(self.corrector.valid_skus))

                # 默认选项逻辑
                default_idx = 0
                if suggestions:
                    try:
                        default_idx = all_valid.index(suggestions[0])
                    except:
                        pass

                target_sku = st.selectbox("选择正确 SKU:", all_valid, index=default_idx, key=f"sel_{idx}")

                if st.button("确认映射", key=f"btn_map_{idx}"):
                    # 修改内存中的 DF
                    st.session_state.inv_df['SKU'] = st.session_state.inv_df['SKU'].replace(bad_sku, target_sku)
                    st.toast(f"已映射: {bad_sku} -> {target_sku}")
                    st.session_state.inv_error_idx += 1
                    time.sleep(0.2)
                    st.rerun()

            # Option B: Create
            with tab_new:
                opts = self.loader.get_category_options()  # Service Call
                with st.form(key=f"frm_new_{idx}"):
                    c1, c2 = st.columns(2)
                    n_sku = c1.text_input("SKU Name", value=bad_sku)
                    n_cat = c2.selectbox("Category", [""] + opts["Category"])

                    c3, c4 = st.columns(2)
                    n_sub = c3.selectbox("SubCategory", [""] + opts["SubCategory"])
                    n_typ = c4.selectbox("Type", [""] + opts["Type"])

                    c5, c6 = st.columns(2)
                    n_cost = c5.number_input("Cost", 0.0, step=0.01)
                    n_frt = c6.number_input("Freight", 0.0, step=0.01)

                    if st.form_submit_button("注册并使用"):
                        # 调用 Service 注册
                        try:
                            self.loader.register_new_sku(n_sku, n_cat, n_sub, n_typ, n_cost, n_frt)
                            # 如果注册的 SKU 和原来的不一样（用户改名了），则更新 DF
                            if n_sku != bad_sku:
                                st.session_state.inv_df['SKU'] = st.session_state.inv_df['SKU'].replace(bad_sku, n_sku)

                            st.success(f"新 SKU {n_sku} 注册成功！")
                            st.session_state.inv_error_idx += 1
                            time.sleep(0.5)
                            st.rerun()
                        except Exception as e:
                            st.error(f"注册失败: {e}")

    # --- Step 3: Commit ---
    def _step_commit(self):
        target_month = st.session_state.inv_target_month
        df = st.session_state.inv_df

        st.success("🎉 所有 SKU 校验完毕！")
        st.metric("准备入库记录数", len(df))
        st.metric("目标月份列", target_month)

        # 检查列是否存在 (Service Call)
        col_exists = self.loader.check_column_exists(target_month)
        if col_exists:
            st.warning(f"⚠️ 警告: 月份列 `{target_month}` 已存在，继续操作将覆盖该列的现有数据！")

        pwd = st.text_input("🔑 请输入操作密码:", type="password")

        if st.button("🚀 执行入库", type="primary", use_container_width=True):
            if pwd != Config.DB_OPERATOR_PWD:
                st.error(" 密码错误")
                return

            with st.status("正在执行同步...", expanded=True) as status:
                status.write("💾 写入数据库...")
                # Service Call
                msg = self.loader.sync_to_db(df, target_month)

                status.write("📦 归档文件...")
                # 重新保存最新的 DF (可能修正过 SKU)
                temp_path = st.session_state.inv_file_path
                df.to_csv(temp_path, index=False)

                self.fs.organize_uploader(inventory_ym=target_month.replace("-", "_"))
                self.fs.archive_all()

                status.update(label=" 全部完成", state="complete")
                st.success(msg)
                time.sleep(2)
                self._reset()

==================== END FILE: ui/components/inventory_wizard.py ====================

==================== START FILE: ui/components/transaction_wizard.py ====================
# ui/components/transaction_wizard.py

import streamlit as st
import time
from pathlib import Path
import traceback

from config import Config
from ui.utils import task_monitor
from core.services.file_service import FileService
from core.services.correction_service import CorrectionService
from core.etl.ingest import TransactionLoader, EarningLoader
from core.etl.parser import TransactionParser
from core.etl.transformer import TransactionTransformer


class TransactionWizard:
    """
    [UI组件] 交易流水线向导 - Enterprise V2.3 (Full UI Lock)

    Fix Log:
    - V2.2: 引入 'etl_processing' 状态锁，防止用户在 ETL 运行时重复点击按钮导致卡死。
    - V2.3: 修复清洗完成后的“继续执行”按钮，增加防止误触变灰机制。
    """

    def __init__(self):
        self.corrector = CorrectionService()
        self.fs = FileService()
        self._init_state()

    def _init_state(self):
        """初始化会话状态"""
        if 'trans_state' not in st.session_state:
            st.session_state.trans_state = 'UPLOAD'
        if 'trans_pending_count' not in st.session_state:
            st.session_state.trans_pending_count = 0
        # [New] 增加运行锁，防止重复点击
        if 'etl_processing' not in st.session_state:
            st.session_state.etl_processing = False

    def _reset_state_callback(self):
        st.session_state.trans_state = 'UPLOAD'
        st.session_state.trans_pending_count = 0
        st.session_state.etl_processing = False

    def _lock_etl(self):
        """[Callback] 点击按钮瞬间锁定 UI"""
        st.session_state.etl_processing = True

    def render(self):
        state = st.session_state.trans_state
        if state == 'UPLOAD':
            self._render_upload_step()
        elif state == 'CLEANING':
            self._render_cleaning_step()

    def _render_upload_step(self):
        st.info("💡 第一步：请上传 eBay 原始报表 (Transaction / Order Earnings)。")

        # 文件上传器
        uploaded_files = st.file_uploader(
            "拖拽或点击上传 CSV 文件",
            type=['csv'],
            accept_multiple_files=True,
            key="trans_uploader"
        )

        # [UI Lock] 按钮状态控制
        # 如果正在处理中，按钮变灰，且文字变化
        is_running = st.session_state.etl_processing
        btn_label = "⏳ 正在执行中..." if is_running else "🚀 启动 ETL 流水线"

        # 渲染按钮 (注意：不再直接在 if st.button 中写逻辑)
        st.button(
            btn_label,
            type="primary",
            use_container_width=True,
            disabled=is_running,  # 核心：根据状态禁用
            on_click=self._lock_etl  # 核心：点击即锁定
        )

        # [Execution Block] 基于状态触发逻辑
        if is_running:
            if not uploaded_files:
                st.error(" 请先上传文件！")
                st.session_state.etl_processing = False  # 释放锁
                # 这里不需要 rerun，因为报错后用户需要操作
                return

            try:
                # --- ETL 流程开始 ---
                with task_monitor("ETL 处理进度监控") as monitor:
                    # 1. 接收文件 (10%)
                    monitor.log("📂 [Step 1/4] 接收文件...")
                    Config.UPLOADER_DIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
                    for f in uploaded_files:
                        with open(Config.UPLOADER_DIR / f.name, "wb") as buffer:
                            buffer.write(f.getbuffer())
                    monitor.update_main_progress(0.1)

                    # 2. 整理 (20%)
                    monitor.log("\n🧹 [Step 2/4] 文件标准化...")
                    self.fs.organize_uploader()
                    monitor.update_main_progress(0.2)

                    # 3. 摄入 (40%)
                    monitor.log("\n📥 [Step 3/4] 数据摄入 (Ingest)...")
                    TransactionLoader().run()
                    EarningLoader().run()
                    monitor.update_main_progress(0.4)

                    # 4. 解析 (60%)
                    monitor.log("\n🧩 [Step 4/4] 智能解析 (Parser)...")
                    parser = TransactionParser()
                    res = parser.run()

                    fixed_cnt = len(res.get('auto_fixed', []))
                    pending_cnt = res.get('pending_count', 0)
                    monitor.log(f"   ->  自动修复: {fixed_cnt} 条")
                    monitor.log(f"   -> 🚩 待人工介入: {pending_cnt} 条")
                    monitor.update_main_progress(0.6)

                    # 5. 转换 (100%)
                    st.session_state.trans_pending_count = pending_cnt

                    if pending_cnt > 0:
                        monitor.log(f"\n⚠️ 发现 {pending_cnt} 个异常数据，转入清洗模式。")
                        time.sleep(1.5)  # 给一点时间展示日志
                        st.session_state.trans_state = 'CLEANING'
                        # 注意：这里不立刻 rerun，而是让 finally 块处理解锁和刷新
                    else:
                        monitor.log("\n 校验通过，进入核心转换引擎...")
                        time.sleep(0.5)
                        self._run_final_transform(monitor)

            except Exception as e:
                st.error(f" 严重错误: {str(e)}")
                # 打印堆栈到 UI 方便调试
                st.code(traceback.format_exc())

            finally:
                # [Critical] 无论成功失败，必须释放锁
                st.session_state.etl_processing = False
                # 强制刷新 UI，恢复按钮状态或跳转页面
                st.rerun()

    def _render_cleaning_step(self):
        count = st.session_state.trans_pending_count
        st.warning(f"⚠️ 数据清洗模式：当前剩余 {count} 条异常记录需要处理。")

        row = self.corrector.get_next_pending_issue()
        if row is None:
            st.balloons()
            st.success("🎉 所有异常已修复！准备继续执行。")

            # --- [Fix Start] 增加按钮防误触机制 ---
            is_running = st.session_state.etl_processing
            btn_label = "⏳ 正在执行中..." if is_running else "🚀 继续执行 (Resume)"

            st.button(
                btn_label,
                type="primary",
                use_container_width=True,
                disabled=is_running,  # 运行时变灰
                on_click=self._lock_etl  # 点击即锁定
            )

            if is_running:
                try:
                    with task_monitor("正在完成剩余步骤...") as monitor:
                        self._run_final_transform(monitor)
                except Exception as e:
                    st.error(f"执行出错: {e}")
                    st.code(traceback.format_exc())
                finally:
                    # [特别注意] 这里只释放锁，不执行 st.rerun()
                    # 原因：如果 Rerun，上面 _run_final_transform 画出的成功信息和"返回开始"按钮会被清空。
                    # 我们希望页面停留在成功状态，直到用户点击"返回开始"。
                    st.session_state.etl_processing = False
            # --- [Fix End] ---

            return

        error_info = self._find_first_bad_sku(row)
        if not error_info:
            # 自愈逻辑：如果找不到错误但被标记了，自动跳过
            self.corrector.mark_as_skipped(row['Order number'])
            st.rerun()
            return

        self._render_fix_card(row, error_info)

    def _render_fix_card(self, row, error_info):
        bad_sku = error_info['bad_sku']
        bad_qty = error_info['bad_qty']

        with st.container(border=True):
            c_head1, c_head2 = st.columns([3, 1])
            with c_head1:
                st.markdown(f"#### 🚩 异常 SKU: `{bad_sku}`")
            with c_head2:
                if st.button("跳过此条", key="btn_skip"):
                    self.corrector.mark_as_skipped(row['Order number'])
                    st.rerun()

            c1, c2 = st.columns(2)
            with c1:
                st.caption("原始标签")
                st.code(row.get('Custom label', ''), language="text")
            with c2:
                st.caption("商品标题")
                st.info(row.get('Item title', '-'))

            st.divider()
            suggestions = self.corrector.get_fuzzy_suggestions(bad_sku)
            opts = suggestions + ["✍️ 手动录入"]
            sel = st.radio("智能推荐:", opts, horizontal=True)

            c_in1, c_in2 = st.columns(2)
            with c_in1:
                final_sku = st.text_input("正确 SKU", value=bad_sku if sel == "✍️ 手动录入" else sel).strip().upper()
            with c_in2:
                final_qty = st.text_input("数量", value=bad_qty).strip()

            if st.button(" 确认修复", type="primary", use_container_width=True):
                # 修复逻辑
                if self.corrector.apply_fix(row['Order number'], error_info['index'], row.get('Custom label', ''),
                                            bad_sku, bad_qty, final_sku, str(int(float(final_qty)))):
                    st.toast(f"已修复: {final_sku}")
                    time.sleep(0.5)
                    st.rerun()
                else:
                    st.error("保存失败")

    def _run_final_transform(self, monitor):
        """执行最后一步转换 (带细粒度进度)"""
        monitor.log("\n⚙️ [Step 5/5] 启动向量化转换引擎 (Vectorized Transformer)...")

        transformer = TransactionTransformer()

        def update_progress(p, msg):
            # 转换阶段占总进度的 30% (0.6 -> 0.9)
            base = 0.6
            scale = 0.3
            real_p = base + (p * scale)
            monitor.update_main_progress(real_p)

        transformer.run(progress_callback=update_progress)

        monitor.log("\n📦 [Final] 文件归档...")
        self.fs.archive_all()

        monitor.update_main_progress(1.0)
        st.balloons()
        st.success(" ETL 任务全部完成！")
        st.markdown("---")
        # 重置按钮，点击后通过回调清理状态
        st.button("🔄 返回开始", on_click=self._reset_state_callback, use_container_width=True)

    def _find_first_bad_sku(self, row):
        for i in range(1, 11):
            s = str(row.get(f'P_SKU{i}', '')).strip().upper()
            q = str(row.get(f'P_Quantity{i}', '')).strip()
            if not s or s == 'NONE': continue
            if not self.corrector.is_valid_sku(s) or not self._is_valid_qty(q):
                return {"index": i, "bad_sku": s, "bad_qty": q}
        return None

    def _is_valid_qty(self, val):
        try:
            return float(val) > 0
        except:
            return False
==================== END FILE: ui/components/transaction_wizard.py ====================


==================== START FILE: ui/components/safety.py ====================
# ui/components/safety.py

import streamlit as st
from typing import Optional, Tuple

from config import Config
from core.auth_service import AuthService
from core.context import get_current_user
from core.logging_config import get_logger


logger = get_logger(__name__)


def _verify_current_user_password(raw_password: str) -> bool:
    """
    校验当前登录用户密码是否正确。

    说明：
    - 通过 AuthService 再做一次认证（不改变登录状态）。
    - 只用来在执行高危操作前做 "二次确认"。
    """
    username = get_current_user()
    if not username:
        st.error("当前未登录，无法完成安全校验。")
        return False

    ok, user_obj, msg = AuthService.authenticate(username, raw_password)
    if not ok:
        logger.warning(
            "Dangerous action password verify failed",
            extra={"user": username, "action": "DANGEROUS_VERIFY_FAIL"}
        )
    return ok


def _verify_operator_password(raw_password: str) -> bool:
    """
    使用独立的运维操作密码进行校验（适用于 DB 级别操作）。

    密码在环境变量 / Config.DB_OPERATOR_PWD 中配置：

        export DB_OPERATOR_PWD=xxxxxx
    """
    if not Config.DB_OPERATOR_PWD:
        st.error(" 系统未配置 DB_OPERATOR_PWD，禁止执行此类高危操作。")
        return False

    return raw_password == Config.DB_OPERATOR_PWD


def confirm_dangerous_action(
    title: str,
    description: str,
    *,
    confirm_phrase: str = "CONFIRM",
    require_current_password: bool = True,
    require_operator_password: bool = False,
    key_prefix: str = "danger_confirm",
) -> Tuple[bool, Optional[str]]:
    """
    高危操作统一确认组件。

    使用方式（在页面里）示例：
        ok, note = confirm_dangerous_action(
            title="⚠️ 你正在执行数据库还原",
            description="该操作会用历史备份覆盖当前数据库，且不可撤销。",
            confirm_phrase="RESTORE",
            require_current_password=True,
            require_operator_password=True,
            key_prefix="restore_db"
        )
        if ok:
            # 执行真正的危险动作
            do_restore()

    参数：
        title:         确认区域标题
        description:   对本次操作的风险说明（会展示给用户看）
        confirm_phrase:要求用户手工输入的确认短语（大小写敏感）
        require_current_password:
                       是否要求输入当前登录账号密码
        require_operator_password:
                       是否要求输入独立的运维操作密码 DB_OPERATOR_PWD
        key_prefix:    用于区分不同确认区域，避免组件 key 冲突

    返回：
        (confirmed, note)
        confirmed: True 表示所有校验通过，可以执行高危操作；
        note     : 用户输入的备注（可写入日志）。
    """
    username = get_current_user() or "-"
    st.markdown(f"### {title}")
    st.warning(description)

    with st.expander("🛡 安全校验 / Security Check", expanded=True):
        # 备注记录
        note = st.text_area(
            "操作备注（可选）：",
            help="建议简单描述本次操作原因，例如：回滚到 11:30 备份以修复错误导入。",
            key=f"{key_prefix}_note",
        )

        # 1) 当前用户密码确认
        current_pwd_ok = True
        current_pwd_input = ""
        if require_current_password:
            current_pwd_input = st.text_input(
                "请输入当前账号密码以确认身份：",
                type="password",
                key=f"{key_prefix}_current_pwd",
            )
            current_pwd_ok = False  # 默认 False，点击按钮时再校验

        # 2) 运维操作密码（独立于用户密码）
        operator_pwd_ok = True
        operator_pwd_input = ""
        if require_operator_password:
            operator_pwd_input = st.text_input(
                "请输入运维操作密码 (DB Operator Password)：",
                type="password",
                key=f"{key_prefix}_operator_pwd",
            )
            operator_pwd_ok = False

        # 3) 人工输入确认短语
        phrase_input = st.text_input(
            f"请在下方输入确认短语：`{confirm_phrase}`，以继续操作：",
            key=f"{key_prefix}_phrase",
        )

        confirmed = False
        if st.button(" 我已知晓风险，仍然要执行该操作", key=f"{key_prefix}_btn", use_container_width=True):
            # 分步校验
            # 3.1 校验当前登录用户密码
            if require_current_password:
                if not current_pwd_input:
                    st.error("请先输入当前账号的密码。")
                    return False, None
                if not _verify_current_user_password(current_pwd_input):
                    st.error("当前账号密码错误，安全校验失败。")
                    return False, None
                current_pwd_ok = True

            # 3.2 校验运维操作密码
            if require_operator_password:
                if not operator_pwd_input:
                    st.error("请先输入运维操作密码。")
                    return False, None
                if not _verify_operator_password(operator_pwd_input):
                    st.error("运维操作密码错误，安全校验失败。")
                    return False, None
                operator_pwd_ok = True

            # 3.3 校验确认短语
            if phrase_input != confirm_phrase:
                st.error(f"确认短语不正确，请输入：`{confirm_phrase}`。")
                return False, None

            # 所有校验通过
            confirmed = True
            st.success(" 安全校验通过，可以执行后续操作。")

            logger.info(
                "Dangerous action confirmed",
                extra={
                    "user": username,
                    "action": "DANGEROUS_CONFIRMED",
                },
            )

        return confirmed, note if confirmed else None


==================== END FILE: ui/components/safety.py ====================

# ui/pages/user_admin.py

import pandas as pd
import streamlit as st
import time

from core.auth_service import AuthService
from core.logging_config import get_logger

logger = get_logger(__name__)

# 权限定义
PERMISSIONS_MAP = {
    "module.home": "🏠 访问首页 (Home)",
    "module.etl": "🔌 上传数据 (ETL)",
    "module.reports": "📊 商业智能报表 (Reports)",
    "module.db_modify": "🛠️ 修改数据库 (Modify Data)",
    "module.db_admin": "🗄️ 数据库运维 (DB Admin)",
    "module.user_admin": "👤 用户管理 (User Admin)",
    "module.audit_logs": "📜 审计日志 (Audit Logs)"
}


def _ensure_admin():
    user = st.session_state.get("auth_user")
    if not user or not user.get("is_admin"):
        st.error(" 权限不足 (Admin Only)")
        st.stop()
    return user


def _load_user_list():
    df = AuthService.list_users()
    if df.empty: return df

    def get_status_icon(row):
        if row["is_locked"]: return "🔴 锁定"
        if row["is_admin"]: return "🛡️ 管理员"
        return "🟢 用户"

    df["状态"] = df.apply(get_status_icon, axis=1)
    return df


def render():
    current_admin = _ensure_admin()

    st.title("👤 用户与权限管理 (User Admin)")
    st.caption("创建新用户、重置密码、配置功能访问权限及查看登录审计。")

    col_list, col_detail = st.columns([1.5, 2.5])

    # --- 左侧列表 ---
    with col_list:
        st.subheader("👥 用户名录")
        df_users = _load_user_list()

        if df_users.empty:
            st.info("暂无用户")
            selected_username = None
        else:
            st.dataframe(
                df_users[["username", "状态", "failed_attempts"]],
                use_container_width=True,
                hide_index=True,
                column_config={
                    "username": "用户名",
                    "failed_attempts": st.column_config.NumberColumn("失败次数", help="连续登录失败次数")
                }
            )
            user_options = df_users["username"].tolist()
            selected_username = st.selectbox("👉 选择要管理的用户:", user_options, key="user_selector")

        st.markdown("---")
        with st.expander("➕ 注册新用户", expanded=False):
            with st.form("create_user_form"):
                new_u = st.text_input("用户名", placeholder="user_new")
                new_p = st.text_input("初始密码", type="password")
                new_is_admin = st.checkbox("设为管理员 (Admin)", value=False)

                if st.form_submit_button("创建用户", type="primary", use_container_width=True):
                    if not new_u or not new_p:
                        st.error("请填写完整信息")
                    else:
                        ok, msg = AuthService.create_user(new_u, new_p, new_is_admin)
                        if ok:
                            st.success(f"用户 {new_u} 创建成功！")
                            time.sleep(1)
                            st.rerun()
                        else:
                            st.error(msg)

    # --- 右侧详情 ---
    with col_detail:
        if not selected_username:
            st.info("👈 请在左侧选择一个用户进行操作。")
            st.stop()

        user_info = df_users[df_users["username"] == selected_username].iloc[0]
        is_self = (selected_username == current_admin.get("username"))

        st.subheader(f"⚙️ 配置: {selected_username}")

        # 1. 状态卡片
        with st.container(border=True):
            c1, c2, c3 = st.columns(3)
            with c1:
                st.metric("账号角色", "管理员" if user_info["is_admin"] else "普通用户")
            with c2:
                st.metric("账号状态", "已锁定" if user_info["is_locked"] else "正常",
                          delta="-锁定" if user_info["is_locked"] else "Active")
            with c3:
                st.metric("登录失败", f"{user_info['failed_attempts']} 次")

            if not is_self:
                if user_info["is_locked"]:
                    if st.button("🔓 解锁账号", use_container_width=True):
                        AuthService.set_lock_state(selected_username, False)
                        st.success("账号已解锁！")
                        time.sleep(0.5)
                        st.rerun()
                else:
                    if st.button("🚫 锁定账号", type="primary", use_container_width=True):
                        AuthService.set_lock_state(selected_username, True)
                        st.warning("账号已锁定！")
                        time.sleep(0.5)
                        st.rerun()

        # 2. [New] 登录行为统计卡片
        stats = AuthService.get_user_login_stats(selected_username)
        with st.container(border=True):
            st.markdown("#### 📊 登录足迹 (Audit Trail)")
            c1, c2 = st.columns(2)
            c1.metric("总登录次数", stats["total_logins"])
            c2.metric("使用过的 IP 数", len(stats["ip_history"]))

            with st.expander("查看 IP 访问详情", expanded=False):
                if not stats["ip_history"].empty:
                    st.dataframe(
                        stats["ip_history"],
                        use_container_width=True,
                        column_config={
                            "ip_address": "IP 地址",
                            "count": st.column_config.NumberColumn("登录次数", format="%d"),
                            "last_seen": st.column_config.DatetimeColumn("最近登录时间", format="YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss")
                        }
                    )
                else:
                    st.caption("暂无登录记录")

        # 3. 密码重置
        with st.expander("🔑 重置密码 (Password Reset)", expanded=False):
            if is_self:
                st.warning("出于安全考虑，请在个人设置页面修改密码（本系统暂未开放自修改）。")
            else:
                new_pwd_input = st.text_input("输入新密码:", key="new_pwd_input", type="password")
                if st.button("确认重置密码", type="secondary"):
                    if new_pwd_input:
                        ok, msg = AuthService.reset_password(selected_username, new_pwd_input)
                        if ok:
                            st.success("密码已重置！请复制下方密码发给用户：")
                            st.code(new_pwd_input, language="text")
                        else:
                            st.error(msg)
                    else:
                        st.error("密码不能为空")

        # 4. 权限设置
        if user_info["is_admin"]:
            st.info("🛡️ 该用户是管理员，默认拥有所有系统权限，无需单独配置。")
        else:
            st.markdown("#### 🔒 权限设置 (Permissions)")
            current_perms = AuthService.get_permissions(selected_username)
            with st.form("perm_form"):
                st.write("请勾选允许访问的模块：")
                new_perms = {}
                cols = st.columns(2)
                for i, (key, label) in enumerate(PERMISSIONS_MAP.items()):
                    is_sensitive = "admin" in key or "modify" in key
                    default_val = current_perms.get(key, False)
                    with cols[i % 2]:
                        new_perms[key] = st.checkbox(label, value=default_val, key=f"perm_{key}")
                        if is_sensitive: st.caption("⚠️ 敏感权限")

                st.markdown("---")
                if st.form_submit_button("💾 保存权限设置", type="primary", use_container_width=True):
                    AuthService.set_permissions(selected_username, new_perms)
                    st.success(f"用户 {selected_username} 的权限已更新！")
                    time.sleep(1)
                    st.rerun()

# ui/pages/home.py

import streamlit as st
import base64
import re
import streamlit.components.v1 as components
from config import Config


def get_base64_encoded_image(image_path):
    try:
        with open(image_path, "rb") as img_file:
            return base64.b64encode(img_file.read()).decode('utf-8')
    except FileNotFoundError:
        return None


def _parse_text_to_html(raw_text):
    """
    [智能解析器 V2.2]
    """
    raw_text = raw_text.strip()

    # 如果已经是 HTML，直接返回
    if re.search(r"<[a-z/]+>", raw_text):
        return raw_text

    lines = [line.strip() for line in raw_text.split('\n') if line.strip()]
    if not lines:
        return ""

    html_parts = []

    # 1. 标题
    title = lines[0].replace("<b>", "").replace("</b>", "")
    html_parts.append(f"<b>{title}</b>")

    # 2. 列表
    rest_lines = lines[1:]
    if rest_lines:
        html_parts.append("<ul>")
        for line in rest_lines:
            content = line.lstrip("-").lstrip("*").strip()
            if "：" in content:
                parts = content.split("：", 1)
                content = f"<b>{parts[0]}：</b>{parts[1]}"
            elif ":" in content:
                if "http" not in content[:4]:
                    parts = content.split(":", 1)
                    content = f"<b>{parts[0]}:</b>{parts[1]}"

            html_parts.append(f"<li>{content}</li>")
        html_parts.append("</ul>")

    return "".join(html_parts)


def render():
    # 1. Logo
    logo_path = Config.ASSETS_DIR / "Logo.png"
    logo_b64 = get_base64_encoded_image(logo_path)

    # 2. CSS (保持样式不变)
    st.markdown("""
        <style>
        .welcome-wrapper {
            display: flex;
            flex-direction: column; align-items: center; justify-content: center;
            height: 70vh; text-align: center; animation: fadeIn 1.2s ease-in-out;
        }
        .big-logo {
            width: 80%;
            max-width: 380px; height: auto; margin-bottom: 30px;
            filter: drop-shadow(0 0 30px rgba(78, 201, 176, 0.15)); transition: transform 0.5s;
        }
        .big-logo:hover { transform: scale(1.02); }
        .welcome-title {
            font-size: 36px; font-weight: 200; color: #FFFFFF; letter-spacing: 4px;
            margin-bottom: 10px; text-shadow: 0 4px 10px rgba(0,0,0,0.5);
        }
        .welcome-subtitle {
            font-size: 16px; color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.5); font-family: 'Consolas', monospace;
            background: rgba(0,0,0,0.3); padding: 8px 20px; border-radius: 20px;
            border: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.05);
        }
        .patch-panel {
            background-color: rgba(25, 25, 25, 0.6);
            border: 1px solid rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1);
            border-top: 3px solid #4EC9B0; border-radius: 6px; 
            height: 65vh; overflow-y: scroll; padding: 0; margin-top: 2vh;
            box-shadow: 0 10px 30px rgba(0,0,0,0.3); backdrop-filter: blur(10px);
            scrollbar-width: none; -ms-overflow-style: none;
        }
        .patch-panel::-webkit-scrollbar { display: none; }
        .patch-header {
            position: sticky; top: 0; background-color: rgba(30, 30, 30, 0.95);
            padding: 15px 20px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.1);
            font-size: 16px; font-weight: 700; color: #4EC9B0;
            display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; z-index: 10;
        }
        .patch-content { padding: 20px; }
        .patch-item {
            margin-bottom: 25px; position: relative; padding-left: 20px;
            border-left: 2px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.1);
        }
        .patch-item::before {
            content: ''; position: absolute; left: -6px; top: 0;
            width: 10px; height: 10px; background: #333; border: 2px solid #4EC9B0; border-radius: 50%;
        }
        .patch-ver {
            display: block; font-size: 15px; font-weight: bold; color: #E0E0E0; margin-bottom: 4px;
        }
        .patch-date { font-size: 12px; color: #666; margin-left: 10px; font-weight: normal; }
        .patch-desc { font-size: 13px; color: #B0B0B0; line-height: 1.6; }
        .patch-desc ul { padding-left: 18px; margin: 5px 0; }
        .patch-desc li { margin-bottom: 4px; }
        .patch-desc b { color: #DCDCDC; font-weight: 700; }
        @keyframes fadeIn { from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(10px); } to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); } }
        </style>
    """, unsafe_allow_html=True)

    # 3. 布局
    col_left, col_right = st.columns([1.4, 1])

    with col_left:
        img_tag = f'<img src="data:image/png;base64,{logo_b64}" class="big-logo">' if logo_b64 else "<h1>🦅</h1>"
        st.markdown(
            f"""<div class="welcome-wrapper">{img_tag}<div class="welcome-title">Eaglestar Pro</div><div class="welcome-subtitle">⬅️ 请在左侧导航栏选择功能模块</div></div>""",
            unsafe_allow_html=True)

    with col_right:
        latest_ver = Config.APP_VERSION
        patch_list = Config.PATCH_NOTES_LIST

        # 强制排序：日期从小到大 (Old -> New)
        if patch_list:
            try:
                patch_list = sorted(patch_list, key=lambda x: x['date'])
            except:
                pass

        items_html = ""
        if not patch_list:
            items_html = "<div style='padding:20px; color:#666;'>暂无更新记录</div>"
        else:
            for note in patch_list:
                formatted_desc = _parse_text_to_html(note['desc'])
                # [Fix] 紧凑拼接，不留换行符，防止 Markdown 误判代码块
                items_html += f'<div class="patch-item"><span class="patch-ver">{note["ver"]} <span class="patch-date">{note["date"]}</span></span><div class="patch-desc">{formatted_desc}</div></div>'

        double_content_html = items_html + items_html if patch_list else items_html

        # [Fix] 紧凑拼接容器 HTML
        final_html = f'<div class="patch-panel" id="auto-scroll-panel"><div class="patch-header"><span>📅 更新日志 (Changelog)</span><span style="font-size:12px; opacity:0.6;">Current: {latest_ver}</span></div><div class="patch-content">{double_content_html}</div></div>'

        st.markdown(final_html, unsafe_allow_html=True)

    # 4. JS 滚动逻辑
    js_code = """
    <script>
        function setupAutoScroll() {
            const panel = window.parent.document.getElementById('auto-scroll-panel');
            if (!panel) { setTimeout(setupAutoScroll, 100); return; }

            let isPaused = false;
            let resumeTimeout = null;
            const speed = 0.3; 
            let scrollAccumulator = panel.scrollTop;

            function step() {
                if (!isPaused) {
                    scrollAccumulator += speed;
                    panel.scrollTop = scrollAccumulator;
                    if (panel.scrollTop >= (panel.scrollHeight / 2)) {
                        scrollAccumulator = 0;
                        panel.scrollTop = 0;
                    }
                } else {
                    scrollAccumulator = panel.scrollTop;
                }
                requestAnimationFrame(step);
            }

            const pause = () => { isPaused = true; if (resumeTimeout) clearTimeout(resumeTimeout); };
            const resume = () => {
                if (resumeTimeout) clearTimeout(resumeTimeout);
                resumeTimeout = setTimeout(() => { isPaused = false; }, 1000);
            };

            panel.addEventListener('mouseenter', pause);
            panel.addEventListener('mouseleave', resume);
            panel.addEventListener('wheel', () => { pause(); resume(); });
            panel.addEventListener('touchstart', pause);
            panel.addEventListener('touchend', resume);

            requestAnimationFrame(step);
        }
        setupAutoScroll();
    </script>
    """
    components.html(js_code, height=0)

==================== END FILE: ui/pages/home.py ====================
