# ui/pages/reports.py

import os
import datetime
import streamlit as st
from typing import List, Tuple, Type
from pathlib import Path
import traceback

# -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
# 1. 核心依赖
# -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
from config import Config
from ui.utils import task_monitor, parse_compound_csv  # [Fix] 引入新解析器

# 引入报表文件管理器
from core.services.report_manager import ReportFileManager

# 引入所有业务分析服务
from core.services.sales_analyzer import SalesQtyAnalyzer
from core.services.profit_sku import SkuProfitAnalyzer
from core.services.profit_listing import ListingProfitAnalyzer
from core.services.profit_combo import ComboProfitAnalyzer
from core.services.crm import CustomerAnalyzer
from core.services.logistics import ShippingAnalyzer
from core.services.prediction import PredictionService
from core.services.ordering import OrderingService
from core.services.inventory_snapshot import InventorySnapshot


class ReportPage:
    """
    [UI层] 商业智能分析报告页面 (BI Reports) - Enterprise V2.2

    升级特性:
    - [Fix] 增加 UI 状态锁，防止按钮在运行中被重复点击。
    - 集成在线报表预览中心 (Report Center)。
    - 支持多表堆叠 CSV 的智能解析。
    """

    def __init__(self):
        self.report_manager = ReportFileManager()
        self._init_state()

        # 定义分析任务清单 (顺序执行)
        self.TASK_REGISTRY = [
            ("📦 SKU 销量统计 (Sales Analysis)", SalesQtyAnalyzer),
            ("💰 SKU 利润与诊断 (SKU Profit)", SkuProfitAnalyzer),
            ("🔗 Listing 表现分析 (Listing Profit)", ListingProfitAnalyzer),
            ("🎁 Combo 策略分析 (Combo Profit)", ComboProfitAnalyzer),
            ("👥 客户画像与风险 (CRM Analysis)", CustomerAnalyzer),
            ("🚚 物流效益诊断 (Logistics)", ShippingAnalyzer),
            ("🤖 AI 销量预测 (AI Prediction)", PredictionService),
            ("🛒 智能补货计算 (Smart Ordering)", OrderingService),
            ("🏦 库存资产快照 (Asset Snapshot)", InventorySnapshot)
        ]

    def _init_state(self):
        """初始化 UI 状态锁"""
        if 'report_processing' not in st.session_state:
            st.session_state.report_processing = False

    def _lock_ui(self):
        """[Callback] 点击即锁定"""
        st.session_state.report_processing = True

    # ... [配置面板代码保持不变] ...
    def _render_config_panel(self) -> dict:
        st.markdown("#### ⚙️ 业务参数配置 (Business Parameters)")
        st.caption("提示: 调整以下参数将直接影响 **净利润** 和 **建议补货量** 的计算结果。")

        with st.expander("展开详细参数设置", expanded=True):
            col_loss, col_supply = st.columns([1.2, 1])

            with col_loss:
                st.markdown("**📉 耗损率标准 (Loss Rates)**")
                lr_case = st.slider("投诉 (Case) 耗损率", 0.0, 1.0, Config.LOSS_RATES.get('CASE', 0.6), 0.01)
                lr_req = st.slider("申请 (Request) 耗损率", 0.0, 1.0, Config.LOSS_RATES.get('REQUEST', 0.5), 0.01)
                lr_ret = st.slider("退货 (Return) 耗损率", 0.0, 1.0, Config.LOSS_RATES.get('RETURN', 0.3), 0.01)
                lr_disp = st.slider("争议 (Dispute) 耗损率", 0.0, 1.0, Config.LOSS_RATES.get('DISPUTE', 1.0), 0.01)

            with col_supply:
                st.markdown("**📦 供应链参数**")
                lead_time = st.number_input("订货提前期 (Lead Month)", min_value=0.0, value=float(Config.LEAD_MONTH),
                                            step=0.1)
                safety_month = st.number_input("最低安全库存 (Safety Month)", min_value=0.0,
                                               value=float(Config.MIN_SAFETY_MONTH), step=0.1)

        return {
            "loss_rates": {"CASE": lr_case, "REQUEST": lr_req, "RETURN": lr_ret, "DISPUTE": lr_disp},
            "lead_time": lead_time,
            "safety_month": safety_month
        }

    # ... [管道逻辑保持不变] ...
    def _run_pipeline(self, start_date: datetime.date, end_date: datetime.date):
        suffix = f"{start_date.strftime('%Y_%m_%d')}->{end_date.strftime('%Y_%m_%d')}"
        total_steps = len(self.TASK_REGISTRY)

        self.report_manager.clear_old_reports()

        with task_monitor(f"🚀 全量分析引擎启动 ({start_date} 至 {end_date})") as monitor:
            for idx, (task_name, ServiceClass) in enumerate(self.TASK_REGISTRY):
                step_index = idx + 1
                progress_pct = idx / total_steps
                monitor.update_main_progress(progress_pct)
                monitor.log(f"\n>>> [Step {step_index}/{total_steps}] 正在执行: {task_name}...")

                try:
                    service_instance = ServiceClass(start_date, end_date, suffix)
                    service_instance.run()
                    monitor.log(f" {task_name} 执行成功。")
                except Exception as e:
                    monitor.log(f" {task_name} 发生严重错误: {str(e)}")
                    monitor.log(traceback.format_exc())

            monitor.update_main_progress(1.0)
            st.session_state.analysis_finished = True

    def _render_report_center(self):
        """[Tab] 报表中心：在线预览与管理"""
        st.info("💡 这里可以直接预览生成的报表，无需下载。支持复杂的多表报表解析。")

        files = self.report_manager.get_generated_files()
        if not files:
            st.warning("暂无报表文件，请先在 [生成报表] 页面运行分析。")
            if st.button("🔄 刷新列表"): st.rerun()
            return

        col_list, col_view = st.columns([1, 3])

        with col_list:
            st.markdown("### 📑 文件列表")
            selected_file = st.radio("选择文件预览:", files, label_visibility="collapsed")

            st.markdown("---")
            # 批量下载/删除
            zip_bytes = self.report_manager.create_zip_archive()
            timestamp = datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M')
            st.download_button(
                "📦 打包下载所有 (.zip)",
                data=zip_bytes,
                file_name=f"Reports_{timestamp}.zip",
                mime="application/zip",
                use_container_width=True
            )

            # 删除按钮也加上防误触
            if st.button("🗑️ 清空所有报表", type="secondary", use_container_width=True):
                self.report_manager.clear_old_reports()
                st.toast("已清空")
                time.sleep(0.5)
                st.rerun()

        with col_view:
            if selected_file:
                file_path = Path(self.report_manager.get_file_path(selected_file))

                st.markdown(f"### 📄 预览: `{selected_file}`")
                with open(file_path, "rb") as fp:
                    st.download_button("📥 下载此文件", fp, file_name=selected_file, mime="text/csv")

                st.divider()

                # [核心调用] 使用智能解析器
                tables = parse_compound_csv(file_path)

                if not tables:
                    st.error("无法解析文件内容或文件为空。")
                else:
                    for title, df in tables:
                        with st.expander(f"📊 {title} ({len(df)} 行)", expanded=True):
                            st.dataframe(df, use_container_width=True)

    def render(self):
        st.title("📊 商业智能报表 (BI Reports)")
        st.caption(f"Enterprise Analytics Engine {Config.APP_VERSION}")

        tab_gen, tab_view = st.tabs(["🚀 生成报表 (Generator)", "📂 报表中心 (Report Center)"])

        # --- Tab 1: 生成 ---
        with tab_gen:
            with st.container(border=True):
                st.markdown("#### 📅 分析周期选择")
                c1, c2 = st.columns(2)
                with c1:
                    today = datetime.date.today()
                    first_day_curr = today.replace(day=1)
                    last_day_prev = first_day_curr - datetime.timedelta(days=1)
                    first_day_prev = last_day_prev.replace(day=1)
                    d_start = st.date_input("开始日期 (Start Date)", first_day_prev)
                with c2:
                    d_end = st.date_input("结束日期 (End Date)", last_day_prev)

            with st.container(border=True):
                params = self._render_config_panel()

            st.markdown("---")

            # 启动逻辑 (含状态锁)
            is_running = st.session_state.report_processing

            # 校验日期
            date_error = (d_start > d_end)
            if date_error:
                st.error("⚠️ 开始日期不能晚于结束日期！")

            # 按钮状态控制
            btn_label = "⏳ 正在分析中..." if is_running else "🚀 确认参数并启动分析"
            btn_disabled = is_running or date_error

            st.button(
                btn_label,
                type="primary",
                use_container_width=True,
                disabled=btn_disabled,
                on_click=self._lock_ui  # 点击即锁定
            )

            # [UI Lock Block] 如果状态为 True，执行逻辑
            if is_running and not date_error:
                try:
                    Config.update_params(
                        lead_time=params["lead_time"],
                        safety_month=params["safety_month"],
                        loss_rates=params["loss_rates"]
                    )
                    st.toast(" 参数已更新，引擎启动中...")
                    st.session_state.analysis_finished = False

                    self._run_pipeline(d_start, d_end)

                    st.balloons()
                    st.success("🎉 所有分析任务执行完毕！请前往 [报表中心] 查看或下载结果。")

                except Exception as e:
                    st.error(f"执行失败: {e}")
                    st.code(traceback.format_exc())

                finally:
                    # [Critical] 释放锁并刷新页面
                    st.session_state.report_processing = False
                    # 稍微延迟一下让用户看到成功的 balloon，然后再 rerun 恢复按钮状态
                    time.sleep(2)
                    st.rerun()

        # --- Tab 2: 查看 ---
        with tab_view:
            self._render_report_center()


def render():
    ReportPage().render()
==================== END FILE: ui/pages/reports.py ====================

# ui/pages/db_data_change.py

import streamlit as st
import pandas as pd
import time
from config import Config
from core.services.data_manager import DataManager
from ui.components.safety import confirm_dangerous_action


def render():
    st.title("🛠️ 数据修改中心 (Data Modification)")
    st.caption("允许授权用户手动修正库存数据或维护 SKU 基础资料。")

    # 初始化 Service
    mgr = DataManager()

    tab_inv, tab_cogs = st.tabs(["📦 修改库存 (Inventory)", "📝 资料维护 (Master Data)"])

    # =========================================================================
    # TAB 1: 修改库存 (Inventory) - 分步向导模式
    # =========================================================================
    with tab_inv:
        # 初始化 Session State
        if 'inv_mod_step' not in st.session_state: st.session_state.inv_mod_step = 1
        if 'inv_mod_date' not in st.session_state: st.session_state.inv_mod_date = None
        if 'inv_mod_sku' not in st.session_state: st.session_state.inv_mod_sku = None

        # --- Step 1: 选择月份 ---
        if st.session_state.inv_mod_step == 1:
            st.info("Step 1/3: 请选择要修改的月份列")
            cols = mgr.get_inventory_columns()

            if not cols:
                st.error("⚠️ 数据库中没有有效的月份列，请先上传库存文件。")
            else:
                sel_date = st.selectbox("选择日期列:", cols)
                if st.button("下一步 ➡️", key="btn_step1"):
                    st.session_state.inv_mod_date = sel_date
                    st.session_state.inv_mod_step = 2
                    st.rerun()

        # --- Step 2: 选择 SKU ---
        elif st.session_state.inv_mod_step == 2:
            st.success(f"当前选中月份: **{st.session_state.inv_mod_date}**")
            st.info("Step 2/3: 请选择要修改的 SKU")

            all_skus = mgr.get_all_skus()
            sel_sku = st.selectbox("选择 SKU (支持搜索):", all_skus)

            c_back, c_next = st.columns([1, 5])
            with c_back:
                if st.button("⬅️ 返回"):
                    st.session_state.inv_mod_step = 1
                    st.rerun()
            with c_next:
                if st.button("下一步 ➡️", key="btn_step2"):
                    st.session_state.inv_mod_sku = sel_sku
                    st.session_state.inv_mod_step = 3
                    st.rerun()

        # --- Step 3: 修改数值并提交 ---
        elif st.session_state.inv_mod_step == 3:
            d = st.session_state.inv_mod_date
            s = st.session_state.inv_mod_sku

            st.markdown(f"#### 🎯 修改目标: `{s}` @ `{d}`")

            # 获取当前值
            curr_val = mgr.get_inventory_value(d, s)

            with st.container(border=True):
                c1, c2 = st.columns(2)
                with c1:
                    st.metric("当前库存", curr_val)
                with c2:
                    new_q = st.number_input("新库存数量", min_value=0, value=curr_val, step=1)

                st.markdown("---")

                # [Security Upgrade] 使用统一安全组件
                confirmed, note = confirm_dangerous_action(
                    title="🔒 安全确认 (Security Check)",
                    description=f"您即将修改历史库存数据。\nSKU: **{s}** | Month: **{d}** | Change: **{curr_val} -> {new_q}**",
                    confirm_phrase="UPDATE",
                    require_current_password=True,
                    require_operator_password=True,
                    key_prefix="inv_mod_confirm"
                )

                if confirmed:
                    ok, msg = mgr.update_inventory_qty(d, s, int(new_q))
                    if ok:
                        st.balloons()
                        st.success(msg)
                        time.sleep(2)
                        # 返回第一步
                        st.session_state.inv_mod_step = 1
                        st.rerun()
                    else:
                        st.error(msg)

            if st.button("⬅️ 取消修改", use_container_width=True):
                st.session_state.inv_mod_step = 2
                st.rerun()

    # =========================================================================
    # TAB 2: 资料维护 (COGS) - 批量编辑 & 新增
    # =========================================================================
    with tab_cogs:
        mode = st.radio("操作模式:", ["📝 批量编辑 (Batch Edit)", "➕ 新增 SKU (Add New)"], horizontal=True)
        st.divider()

        # 准备下拉选项
        opt_cats = [""] + mgr.get_distinct_values('Category')
        opt_subs = [""] + mgr.get_distinct_values('SubCategory')
        opt_types = [""] + mgr.get_distinct_values('Type')

        # --- Mode A: 批量编辑 ---
        if mode == "📝 批量编辑 (Batch Edit)":
            st.info("💡 说明: 可直接在下方表格中修改 Cost 或 Freight，系统会自动计算 Cog。")

            # 加载数据
            if 'df_cogs_edit' not in st.session_state:
                st.session_state.df_cogs_edit = mgr.get_cogs_data()

            # 编辑器
            edited_df = st.data_editor(
                st.session_state.df_cogs_edit,
                key="cogs_editor",
                use_container_width=True,
                height=500,
                column_config={
                    "SKU": st.column_config.TextColumn("SKU", disabled=True),
                    "Cog": st.column_config.NumberColumn("Cog (Auto)", disabled=True, format="%.2f"),
                    "Cost": st.column_config.NumberColumn("Cost", min_value=0, format="%.2f", required=True),
                    "Freight": st.column_config.NumberColumn("Freight", min_value=0, format="%.2f", required=True),
                    "Category": st.column_config.SelectboxColumn("Category", options=opt_cats),
                    "SubCategory": st.column_config.SelectboxColumn("SubCategory", options=opt_subs),
                    "Type": st.column_config.SelectboxColumn("Type", options=opt_types),
                },
                hide_index=True
            )

            # 即时计算
            recalc_cog = (pd.to_numeric(edited_df['Cost'], errors='coerce').fillna(0) +
                          pd.to_numeric(edited_df['Freight'], errors='coerce').fillna(0)).round(2)

            if not edited_df['Cog'].equals(recalc_cog):
                edited_df['Cog'] = recalc_cog
                st.session_state.df_cogs_edit = edited_df
                st.rerun()

            # [Security Upgrade] 批量更新确认
            st.markdown("### 💾 提交更改")

            confirmed, note = confirm_dangerous_action(
                title="🔒 同步确认",
                description="您正在批量修改 SKU 基础资料 (Master Data)。\n请确保已核对所有成本变更。",
                confirm_phrase="SYNC",
                require_current_password=True,
                require_operator_password=True,
                key_prefix="cogs_batch_confirm"
            )

            if confirmed:
                with st.spinner("正在同步..."):
                    ok, msg = mgr.update_cogs_batch(edited_df)
                if ok:
                    st.success(msg)
                    st.balloons()
                    # 强制刷新缓存
                    st.session_state.df_cogs_edit = mgr.get_cogs_data()
                    time.sleep(1.5)
                    st.rerun()
                else:
                    st.error(msg)

        # --- Mode B: 新增 SKU ---
        else:
            st.markdown("#### 🆕 录入新产品")
            st.warning("⚠️ 注意: 新增 SKU 会自动同步到库存表，所有历史月份库存默认为 0。")

            with st.container(border=True):
                c1, c2, c3 = st.columns(3)
                with c1:
                    n_sku = st.text_input("SKU (必填, 唯一)", placeholder="例如: AA-1234").strip()
                with c2:
                    n_cat = st.selectbox("Category", opt_cats, key="new_cat")
                with c3:
                    n_sub = st.selectbox("SubCategory", opt_subs, key="new_sub")

                c4, c5, c6 = st.columns(3)
                with c4:
                    n_type = st.selectbox("Type", opt_types, key="new_type")
                with c5:
                    n_cost = st.number_input("Cost", min_value=0.0, step=0.01, format="%.2f")
                with c6:
                    n_frt = st.number_input("Freight", min_value=0.0, step=0.01, format="%.2f")

                st.info(f"💰 预计 Cog: **{(n_cost + n_frt):.2f}**")
                st.markdown("---")

                # [Security Upgrade] 新增 SKU 确认
                confirmed, note = confirm_dangerous_action(
                    title="🔒 创建确认",
                    description=f"即将创建新 SKU: **{n_sku}**。\n此操作将影响库存表结构。",
                    confirm_phrase="CREATE",
                    require_current_password=True,
                    require_operator_password=True,
                    key_prefix="sku_create_confirm"
                )

                if confirmed:
                    if not n_sku:
                        st.error(" SKU 不能为空")
                    else:
                        data = {
                            "SKU": n_sku, "Category": n_cat, "SubCategory": n_sub,
                            "Type": n_type, "Cost": n_cost, "Freight": n_frt
                        }
                        with st.spinner("正在写入..."):
                            ok, msg = mgr.add_new_sku(data)

                        if ok:
                            st.success(msg)
                            st.balloons()
                            # 清理编辑缓存
                            if 'df_cogs_edit' in st.session_state:
                                del st.session_state.df_cogs_edit
                            time.sleep(1.5)
                            st.rerun()
                        else:
                            st.error(msg)
==================== END FILE: ui/pages/db_data_change.py ====================

# ui/pages/db_admin.py

import os
import re
import time
from datetime import datetime
from typing import List, Dict, Tuple

import streamlit as st

# 确保 Config 被正确导入
from config import Config
from core.services.database_service import DatabaseService
from ui.components.safety import confirm_dangerous_action


def parse_filename_to_display(filename: str) -> str:
    """
    [UI辅助] 解析备份文件名 -> 人类可读格式
    Input:  20251205_174730_init.sql
    Output: 🕒 2025-12-05 17:47:30 | 🏷️ init
    """
    # 去掉路径，只取文件名
    filename = os.path.basename(filename)

    # 去掉扩展名
    base = filename.rsplit(".", 1)[0]
    parts = base.split("_", 2)

    if len(parts) >= 2:
        date_str, time_str = parts[0], parts[1]
        tag = parts[2] if len(parts) > 2 else ""

        # 严格校验是否为数字，防止解析非标准文件报错
        if date_str.isdigit() and time_str.isdigit():
            try:
                dt = datetime.strptime(date_str + time_str, "%Y%m%d%H%M%S")
                time_label = dt.strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")

                if tag:
                    return f"🕒 {time_label} | 🏷️ {tag}"
                else:
                    return f"🕒 {time_label}"
            except:
                pass

    # 如果解析失败，为了安全，不显示原始文件名，显示"未知备份"
    return "❓ 未知格式备份 (Unknown Backup)"


def _build_backup_options(file_list: List[str]) -> Tuple[List[str], Dict[str, str]]:
    """
    构建下拉菜单选项
    Returns: (UI显示列表, 映射字典{显示名: 物理文件名})
    """
    options_map = {}
    for f in file_list:
        display_name = parse_filename_to_display(f)
        # 如果有重复的时间点（极少见），追加后缀防止字典Key冲突
        if display_name in options_map:
            display_name += " (Copy)"
        options_map[display_name] = f

    # 按标签排序 (时间倒序，最新的在前面)
    sorted_labels = sorted(options_map.keys(), reverse=True)
    return sorted_labels, options_map


def render():
    st.title("🗄️ 数据库运维中心 (DB Admin)")
    st.caption("提供数据库快照备份、灾难恢复及环境重置功能。")

    service = DatabaseService()

    tab_backup, tab_restore, tab_manage, tab_danger = st.tabs([
        "📤 创建备份 (Backup)",
        "📥 灾难恢复 (Restore)",
        "🗂️ 备份管理 (Manage)",
        "☢️ 危险区域 (Danger Zone)"
    ])

    # =========================================================================
    # Tab 1: 创建备份
    # =========================================================================
    with tab_backup:
        st.info("💡 说明：此操作将为当前数据库的所有表创建全量快照 (System Snapshot)。")

        with st.container(border=True):
            c1, c2 = st.columns([3, 1])
            with c1:
                tag = st.text_input("快照备注 (可选)", placeholder="例如: Version_1.5_Update")
            with c2:
                st.write("")
                st.write("")
                if st.button("📸 立即备份", type="primary", use_container_width=True):
                    with st.spinner("正在生成快照..."):
                        ok, msg = service.create_backup(tag)
                    if ok:
                        st.success(msg)  # msg 在 service 层已经脱敏，只报大小
                        time.sleep(1)
                        st.rerun()
                    else:
                        st.error(msg)

    # =========================================================================
    # Tab 2: 灾难恢复 (安全脱敏)
    # =========================================================================
    with tab_restore:
        st.warning("⚠️ **高危警告**：还原操作将 **完全覆盖** 当前数据库，且不可撤销！")

        files = service.list_backups()
        if not files:
            st.info("暂无可用还原点。")
        else:
            labels, map_files = _build_backup_options(files)

            selected_label = st.selectbox("请选择还原时间点:", labels)
            # 获取物理文件名用于后端操作，但在前端隐藏
            real_filename = map_files[selected_label]

            st.divider()

            # [Fix] 安全组件：描述中使用 selected_label (格式化时间)，而非 real_filename
            confirmed, note = confirm_dangerous_action(
                title="🔴 最终确认：执行数据库回滚",
                description=f"即将还原至时间点: **{selected_label}**。\n请确认当前没有其他用户正在操作。",
                confirm_phrase="RESTORE",
                require_current_password=True,
                require_operator_password=True,
                key_prefix="db_restore"
            )

            if confirmed:
                progress_bar = st.progress(0.0, text="准备开始还原...")

                def update_ui(p):
                    progress_bar.progress(max(0.0, min(p, 1.0)), text=f"还原进度: {int(p * 100)}%")

                # 传递真实文件名给后端
                ok, msg = service.restore_backup_with_progress(real_filename, update_ui)

                if ok:
                    st.balloons()
                    st.success(f" 数据库已成功回滚至: {selected_label}")
                else:
                    st.error(msg)

    # =========================================================================
    # Tab 3: 备份管理 (安全脱敏)
    # =========================================================================
    with tab_manage:
        files = service.list_backups()
        if not files:
            st.info("暂无历史备份。")
        else:
            st.markdown("#### 🗑️ 历史快照管理")

            # [Fix] 表格展示：列出解析后的时间点，隐藏物理文件名
            df_files = []
            for f in files:
                try:
                    f_path = Config.BACKUP_DIR / f
                    size_kb = os.path.getsize(f_path) / 1024
                    display_name = parse_filename_to_display(f)

                    df_files.append({
                        "备份时间点 / 备注": display_name,
                        "文件大小": f"{size_kb:.1f} KB"
                    })
                except:
                    pass

            st.dataframe(df_files, use_container_width=True)
            st.markdown("---")

            # 删除操作区
            labels, map_files = _build_backup_options(files)
            target_label = st.selectbox("选择要删除的备份:", labels, key="del_sel")
            target_file = map_files[target_label]

            # [Fix] 按钮文本只显示时间点
            if st.button(f"🗑️ 删除: {target_label}", type="secondary"):
                ok, msg = service.delete_backup(target_file)
                if ok:
                    st.toast(f"已删除备份点: {target_label}")
                    time.sleep(1)
                    st.rerun()
                else:
                    st.error(msg)

    # =========================================================================
    # Tab 4: 危险区域 (Reset)
    # =========================================================================
    with tab_danger:
        st.error("💀 **极度危险区**：以下操作具有破坏性，请谨慎执行。")

        with st.container(border=True):
            st.markdown("#### 🧹 一键清空测试数据 (Reset Environment)")
            st.markdown(
                """
                此操作将 **永久清空** 以下业务数据表，仅保留用户账号和 SKU 基础资料：
                - 交易流水 (Transaction)
                - 资金流水 (Order Earning)
                - 报表源数据 (Clean Log)
                - 库存数据 (Inventory)
                """
            )

            confirmed, note = confirm_dangerous_action(
                title="⚠️ 确认清空业务数据",
                description="此操作不可撤销！建议先在 [备份] 页面创建一个快照。",
                confirm_phrase="RESET",
                require_current_password=True,
                require_operator_password=True,
                key_prefix="db_reset"
            )

            if confirmed:
                with st.spinner("正在重置数据库环境..."):
                    ok, msg = service.reset_business_data()

                if ok:
                    st.success(msg)
                    st.balloons()
                else:
                    st.error(msg)

==================== END FILE: ui/pages/db_admin.py ====================


==================== START FILE: ui/pages/audit_logs.py ====================
# ui/pages/audit_logs.py
"""
安全审计日志查看页面 (Audit Logs Center) - Enterprise V2.3

Fix Log:
- UI增强: 在审计列表中显式增加 "来源 IP (Source IP)" 列，实现完整的操作溯源。
"""

from pathlib import Path
from typing import List, Dict, Any
import pandas as pd
import streamlit as st

from config import Config
from core.logging_config import get_logger

logger = get_logger(__name__)


# ==============================================================================
# 权限校验
# ==============================================================================
def _ensure_admin():
    user = st.session_state.get("auth_user")
    if not user or not user.get("is_admin"):
        st.error(" 权限不足：仅管理员可查看审计日志。")
        st.stop()
    return user


# ==============================================================================
# 日志解析引擎
# ==============================================================================
def _parse_log_line(line: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    解析标准日志格式:
    YYYY-MM-DD ... | user=X | action=Y | ... | ip=Z | Message
    """
    line = line.strip()
    if not line: return {}

    # 格式参考 core/logging_config.py
    # 使用 " | " 分割，最后一部分是 message
    parts = line.split(" | ")

    if len(parts) < 4:
        return {"time": "-", "level": "-", "user": "-", "ip": "-", "action": "-", "message": line}

    try:
        ts = parts[0].strip()
        level = parts[1].strip()
        module = parts[2].strip()

        message = parts[-1]
        kv_parts = parts[3:-1]  # 中间部分是键值对

        meta = {}
        for item in kv_parts:
            if "=" in item:
                k, v = item.split("=", 1)
                meta[k.strip()] = v.strip()

        return {
            "time": ts,
            "level": level,
            "module": module,
            "user": meta.get("user", "-"),
            "ip": meta.get("ip", "-"),  # 提取 IP
            "action": meta.get("action", "-"),
            "table": meta.get("table", "-"),
            "message": message,
            "raw": line
        }
    except:
        return {"time": "-", "level": "-", "user": "-", "ip": "-", "message": line}


def _load_logs(log_file: str, max_lines: int = 1000) -> pd.DataFrame:
    path = Path(Config.LOG_DIR) / log_file
    if not path.exists():
        return pd.DataFrame()

    try:
        with path.open("r", encoding="utf-8", errors="ignore") as f:
            lines = f.readlines()[-max_lines:]
        lines.reverse()
        parsed_data = [_parse_log_line(l) for l in lines]
        return pd.DataFrame(parsed_data)
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"读取日志失败: {e}")
        return pd.DataFrame()


# ==============================================================================
# 页面渲染
# ==============================================================================
def render():
    _ensure_admin()
    st.title("📜 安全审计日志 (Audit Logs)")
    st.caption("追踪系统内的所有敏感操作与数据变更，包含操作人 IP 溯源。")

    # --- 过滤器 ---
    with st.container(border=True):
        c1, c2, c3 = st.columns([1, 1, 1])
        with c1:
            log_source = st.radio("日志来源:", ["📢 业务操作日志 (Business)", "🛡️ 数据库底层日志 (DB Kernel)"])
        with c2:
            show_read = st.checkbox("显示只读操作 (SELECT/READ)", value=False)
        with c3:
            limit = st.select_slider("加载行数:", options=[100, 500, 1000, 2000], value=500)

    # --- 加载 ---
    filename = "app.log" if "Business" in log_source else "db_audit.log"
    with st.spinner(f"正在加载 {filename} ..."):
        df = _load_logs(filename, limit)

    if df.empty:
        st.info("暂无日志记录。")
        return

    # --- 过滤 ---
    df = df[df["action"] != "-"]
    if not show_read:
        mask_read = df["action"].str.upper().str.contains("READ|SELECT", na=False)
        df = df[~mask_read]

    search_term = st.text_input("🔍 搜索 (支持 User / IP / Action / Content):", placeholder="例如: 192.168 或 UPDATE")
    if search_term:
        mask_search = df.apply(lambda x: x.astype(str).str.contains(search_term, case=False).any(), axis=1)
        df = df[mask_search]

    st.markdown(f"**共找到 {len(df)} 条记录**")

    # --- [Fix] 表格展示：加入 IP 列 ---
    if "Business" in log_source:
        cols = ["time", "user", "ip", "action", "message"]
    else:
        cols = ["time", "user", "ip", "action", "table", "message"]

    st.dataframe(
        df[cols],
        use_container_width=True,
        hide_index=True,
        column_config={
            "time": st.column_config.TextColumn("时间", width="medium"),
            "user": st.column_config.TextColumn("操作人", width="small"),
            "ip": st.column_config.TextColumn("来源 IP", width="medium"),  # 新增列
            "action": st.column_config.TextColumn("动作", width="small"),
            "table": st.column_config.TextColumn("表名", width="small"),
            "message": st.column_config.TextColumn("详细内容 (Details)", width="large"),
        }
    )

    with st.expander("查看原始数据 (CSV Export)"):
        st.code(df.to_csv(index=False), language="csv")

==================== END FILE: ui/pages/audit_logs.py ====================


==================== START FILE: ui/pages/etl_cleaning.py ====================
# ui/pages/etl_cleaning.py

import streamlit as st
import time
from core.services.correction_service import CorrectionService


class DataCleaningPage:
    """
    [UI层] 数据清洗向导 (Data Cleaning Wizard) - Refactored V2.0

    架构变更:
    - 移除了直接的 DB 访问 (Raw SQL)。
    - 移除了直接的 ETL Parser 调用。
    - 所有业务逻辑代理给 CorrectionService。
    """

    def __init__(self):
        # 仅依赖 Service，不依赖 Repository 或 ETL
        self.corrector = CorrectionService()

    def _find_first_bad_sku(self, row) -> dict:
        """在行中定位第一个错误的字段 (UI 辅助逻辑)"""
        for i in range(1, 11):
            sku_col = f'P_SKU{i}'
            qty_col = f'P_Quantity{i}'

            # 兼容旧版本列名 (虽然 Service 层应该处理，但 UI 层做个防御)
            if sku_col not in row and f"P_SKU{i}" in row:
                sku_col = f"P_SKU{i}"
                qty_col = f"P_Quantity{i}"

            if sku_col not in row: continue

            sku_val = str(row[sku_col]).strip().upper()
            qty_val = str(row[qty_col]).strip()

            # 跳过空数据
            if not sku_val or sku_val == 'NONE': continue

            # 检查 SKU 是否有效 (调用 Service)
            is_sku_valid = self.corrector.is_valid_sku(sku_val)

            # 检查 数量 是否有效 (调用 Service 辅助方法)
            is_qty_valid = self.corrector.validate_quantity(qty_val)

            # 只要有一个无效，就返回该组索引
            if not is_sku_valid or not is_qty_valid:
                return {
                    "index": i,
                    "bad_sku": sku_val,
                    "bad_qty": qty_val,
                    "is_sku_error": not is_sku_valid,
                    "is_qty_error": not is_qty_valid
                }
        return None

    def render(self):
        st.subheader("🛠️ 数据清洗向导 (Data Cleaning Wizard)")

        col1, col2 = st.columns([3, 1])
        with col1:
            st.info("️ 系统将引导您逐个修复异常数据。您的选择将被系统记忆，下次自动应用。")
        with col2:
            if st.button("🔄 重新扫描全库", use_container_width=True):
                with st.spinner("🔄 正在重新扫描与自动修复..."):
                    # [调用 Service] 运行解析器
                    report = self.corrector.run_auto_parser()

                logs = report.get("auto_fixed", [])
                pending = report.get("pending_count", 0)

                if logs:
                    st.success(f" 自动修复了 {len(logs)} 个历史问题！")
                    with st.expander("查看修复详情", expanded=False):
                        for log in logs:
                            st.markdown(f"- 订单 `{log['order']}`: {log['msg']}")
                elif pending == 0:
                    st.success("🎉 数据已全部清洗完毕！")
                else:
                    st.info(f"扫描完成，剩余 {pending} 个待处理项。")

                time.sleep(1)
                st.rerun()

        # 1. 获取异常数据 (调用 Service)
        row = self.corrector.get_next_pending_issue()

        if row is None:
            st.balloons()
            st.success("🎉 所有异常数据处理完毕！您可以进行下一步分析了。")
            return

        error_info = self._find_first_bad_sku(row)

        # 自愈机制: 如果标记了错误但找不到错，调用 Service 标记跳过
        if not error_info:
            self.corrector.mark_as_skipped(row['Order number'])
            st.rerun()
            return

        # 2. 提取上下文信息
        bad_sku = error_info['bad_sku']
        bad_qty = error_info['bad_qty']
        is_sku_error = error_info['is_sku_error']
        is_qty_error = error_info['is_qty_error']

        order_id = row['Order number']
        label = row['Custom label']
        title = row['Item title']

        # 3. 渲染界面
        with st.container(border=True):
            # 顶部信息栏
            st.markdown(f"### 🚩 发现异常: `{bad_sku}` (Qty: {bad_qty})")

            c_info1, c_info2 = st.columns(2)
            with c_info1:
                st.caption("Custom Label (原始标签)")
                st.code(label, language="text")
            with c_info2:
                st.caption("Item Title (商品标题)")
                st.info(title)

            st.divider()

            # --- 核心交互区 ---
            st.markdown("#### 🔧 选择修复方式")

            # A. 准备选项 (调用 Service 获取建议)
            suggestions = self.corrector.get_fuzzy_suggestions(bad_sku)

            radio_options = [s for s in suggestions]
            manual_option_label = "✍️ 手动录入 (Manual Input)"
            radio_options.append(manual_option_label)

            # B. 渲染单选框
            selected_option = st.radio(
                "请选择正确的数据:",
                options=radio_options,
                index=0,
                horizontal=False
            )

            st.markdown("---")

            # C. 动态输入区
            final_sku = None
            final_qty = None
            can_submit = False

            # 分支 1: 用户选择了 "手动录入"
            if selected_option == manual_option_label:
                c_in1, c_in2 = st.columns(2)

                with c_in1:
                    if is_sku_error:
                        input_sku = st.text_input("正确 SKU", value="", placeholder="请输入 Data_COGS 中存在的 SKU")
                    else:
                        input_sku = st.text_input("SKU (无需修改)", value=bad_sku, disabled=True)

                with c_in2:
                    if is_qty_error:
                        input_qty = st.text_input("正确数量", value="1")
                    else:
                        input_qty = st.text_input("数量 (无需修改)", value=bad_qty, disabled=True)

                final_sku = input_sku.strip().upper()
                final_qty = input_qty.strip()
                can_submit = True

            # 分支 2: 用户选择了 "智能推荐"
            else:
                final_sku = selected_option
                if is_qty_error:
                    final_qty = "1"
                    st.caption(f"💡 原数量 `{bad_qty}` 无效，智能修复将默认设为 `1`。")
                else:
                    final_qty = bad_qty
                can_submit = True

            # D. 提交按钮与处理
            if can_submit:
                if st.button(" 确认并修复 (Confirm & Fix)", type="primary", use_container_width=True):
                    # 最终校验逻辑
                    errors = []

                    # 校验 SKU
                    if not final_sku:
                        errors.append("SKU 不能为空")
                    elif not self.corrector.is_valid_sku(final_sku):
                        errors.append(f"SKU `{final_sku}` 无效 (未在 Data_COGS 中找到)")

                    # 校验 Quantity
                    if not self.corrector.validate_quantity(final_qty):
                        errors.append(f"数量 `{final_qty}` 无效 (必须是大于0的整数)")

                    if errors:
                        for e in errors:
                            st.error(f" {e}")
                    else:
                        clean_qty = str(int(float(final_qty)))
                        # [调用 Service] 提交修复
                        success = self.corrector.apply_fix(
                            order_id, error_info['index'],
                            label, bad_sku, bad_qty,
                            final_sku, clean_qty
                        )

                        if success:
                            st.toast(f" 已修正: {final_sku} x {clean_qty}")
                            time.sleep(0.5)
                            st.rerun()
                        else:
                            st.error(" 数据库更新失败，请查看日志。")


def render():
    DataCleaningPage().render()
==================== END FILE: ui/pages/etl_cleaning.py ====================


==================== START FILE: ui/pages/data_visualization.py ====================
# ui/pages/data_visualization.py

import streamlit as st
import datetime
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
import altair as alt
from config import Config
from core.services.visual_service import VisualService

# --- MAPPING DICTIONARIES (New Chinese Names) ---
ACTION_MAP_UI_TO_DB = {
    "产品销售": "Sales", "订单取消": "Cancel", "无平台介入主动退货": "Return",
    "平台介入用户退货": "Request", "平台介入强制退货": "Case", "第三方仅退款": "Dispute"
}
ACTION_MAP_DB_TO_UI = {v: k for k, v in ACTION_MAP_UI_TO_DB.items()}

SHIP_MAP_UI_TO_DB = {
    "普通邮递": "ShipRegular", "邮费罚款": "ShipUnder",
    "邮费超支": "ShipOver", "包退货邮费": "ShipReturn"
}

FEE_MAP_UI_TO_DB = {
    "产品成本": "COGS", "平台费用": "PlatformFee"
}


@st.cache_resource
def get_visual_service_v7():
    return VisualService()


@st.cache_data(ttl=600)
def load_data_v6(start_date, end_date, stores):
    service = get_visual_service_v7()
    return service.load_and_aggregate(start_date, end_date, stores)


def render():
    st.title("📈 数据交互可视化 (Interactive Visualization)")
    st.caption(f"Enterprise 3D Analytics Cockpit {Config.APP_VERSION}")

    st.markdown("""
        <style>
        .block-container { padding-top: 2rem !important; padding-bottom: 2rem !important; }
        .control-panel {
            background-color: rgba(30, 30, 40, 0.8);
            padding: 20px;
            border-radius: 12px;
            border: 1px solid rgba(78, 201, 176, 0.3);
            box-shadow: 0 0 20px rgba(0,0,0,0.5);
        }
        div[data-testid="stRadio"] > label { font-weight: bold; color: #4EC9B0; }
        </style>
    """, unsafe_allow_html=True)

    with st.container():
        c_title, c_clear = st.columns([5, 1])
        with c_title: pass
        with c_clear:
            if st.button("🧹 强制刷新"):
                st.cache_data.clear()
                st.cache_resource.clear()
                st.rerun()

        c1, c2, c3 = st.columns([1.5, 2, 1])
        with c1:
            st.markdown("### 👁️ 统计方式 (Method)")
            view_mode = st.radio(
                "View Mode",
                ["Amount", "Quantity", "Order", "Percentage"],
                horizontal=True,
                label_visibility="collapsed"
            )
        with c2:
            st.markdown("### 📅 时间区间 (Time Range)")
            end_def = datetime.date.today()
            start_def = end_def - datetime.timedelta(days=30)
            date_range = st.date_input("Select Range", value=(start_def, end_def), label_visibility="collapsed")
        with c3:
            st.markdown("### 🏪 店铺 (Store)")
            stores = st.multiselect("Stores", ["esplus", "88"], default=["esplus", "88"], label_visibility="collapsed")

    st.markdown("---")

    col_filters, col_main = st.columns([1, 3.5])

    disable_ship_filters = (view_mode == "Quantity")
    disable_fee_filters = (view_mode == "Quantity") or (view_mode == "Order")

    action_ui_list = list(ACTION_MAP_UI_TO_DB.keys())
    ship_ui_list = list(SHIP_MAP_UI_TO_DB.keys())
    fee_ui_list = list(FEE_MAP_UI_TO_DB.keys())

    with col_filters:
        st.markdown('<div class="control-panel">', unsafe_allow_html=True)
        st.markdown("#### 🛠️ 高级筛选 (Filters)")

        with st.expander("📦 销售类型 (Sales Type)", expanded=True):
            actions = st.multiselect("Action Types", action_ui_list, default=[ACTION_MAP_DB_TO_UI["Sales"]])

        with st.expander("🚚 邮费类型 (Shipping)", expanded=False):
            if disable_ship_filters:
                st.caption("🚫 该模式下不可用")
                ship_types = []
            else:
                ship_types = st.multiselect("Shipping Types", ship_ui_list, default=[])

        with st.expander("💸 销售费用 (Fees)", expanded=False):
            if disable_fee_filters:
                st.caption("🚫 该模式下不可用")
                fees = []
            else:
                fees = st.multiselect("Fee Types", fee_ui_list, default=[])

        st.info(f"模式: {view_mode}")
        st.markdown('</div>', unsafe_allow_html=True)

    df_agg = pd.DataFrame()

    if len(date_range) == 2 and stores:
        start, end = date_range
        with st.spinner("🚀 正在执行向量化聚合计算..."):
            try:
                result = load_data_v6(start, end, stores)
                if isinstance(result, tuple) and len(result) == 2:
                    df_agg, _ = result  # 忽略 SQL
                elif isinstance(result, pd.DataFrame):
                    df_agg = result
                else:
                    st.error(" 数据格式错误")
            except Exception as e:
                st.error(f"Error: {e}")

    with col_main:
        if df_agg.empty:
            st.warning("无数据。请检查时间范围或店铺。")
        else:
            st.success(f" 计算完成 ({len(df_agg)} 行)")

            show_cols = []

            # --- Percentage Mode ---
            if view_mode == "Percentage":
                denom_col = "Sales_Amount"
                if denom_col not in df_agg.columns:
                    denom = pd.Series(0.0)
                else:
                    denom = df_agg[denom_col].replace(0, np.nan)

                for act_ui in actions:
                    act_db = ACTION_MAP_UI_TO_DB.get(act_ui, act_ui)
                    num_col = f"{act_db}_Amount"
                    if num_col in df_agg.columns:
                        pct_col_ui = f"{act_ui} 占比"
                        df_agg[pct_col_ui] = (df_agg[num_col] / denom).fillna(0)
                        show_cols.append(pct_col_ui)

                for ship_ui in ship_types:
                    key_db = SHIP_MAP_UI_TO_DB.get(ship_ui, ship_ui)
                    num_col = f"Total_{key_db}"
                    if num_col in df_agg.columns:
                        pct_col_ui = f"{ship_ui} 占比"
                        df_agg[pct_col_ui] = (df_agg[num_col] / denom).fillna(0)
                        show_cols.append(pct_col_ui)

                for fee_ui in fees:
                    key_db = FEE_MAP_UI_TO_DB.get(fee_ui, fee_ui)
                    num_col = f"Total_{key_db}"
                    if num_col in df_agg.columns:
                        pct_col_ui = f"{fee_ui} 占比"
                        df_agg[pct_col_ui] = (df_agg[num_col] / denom).fillna(0)
                        show_cols.append(pct_col_ui)

            # --- Standard Modes ---
            else:
                suffix = view_mode
                for act_ui in actions:
                    act_db = ACTION_MAP_UI_TO_DB.get(act_ui, act_ui)
                    col = f"{act_db}_{suffix}"
                    if col in df_agg.columns:
                        df_agg[act_ui] = df_agg[col]
                        show_cols.append(act_ui)

                if not disable_ship_filters:
                    prefix = "Total_Order" if view_mode == "Order" else "Total"
                    for ship_ui in ship_types:
                        key_db = SHIP_MAP_UI_TO_DB.get(ship_ui, ship_ui)
                        col = f"{prefix}_{key_db}"
                        if col in df_agg.columns:
                            df_agg[ship_ui] = df_agg[col]
                            show_cols.append(ship_ui)

                if not disable_fee_filters:
                    for fee_ui in fees:
                        key_db = FEE_MAP_UI_TO_DB.get(fee_ui, fee_ui)
                        col = f"Total_{key_db}"
                        if col in df_agg.columns:
                            df_agg[fee_ui] = df_agg[col]
                            show_cols.append(fee_ui)

            # --- Chart Rendering (Altair) ---
            if show_cols:
                # 准备数据
                df_chart = df_agg[['DateStr'] + show_cols].rename(columns={'DateStr': '日期'})
                df_chart_melt = df_chart.melt('日期', var_name='指标', value_name='数值')

                # 设置 Y 轴格式
                if view_mode == "Amount":
                    y_format = '$.2s';
                    y_title = "金额 ($)"
                elif view_mode == "Percentage":
                    y_format = '.1%';
                    y_title = "占比 (%)"
                elif view_mode == "Quantity":
                    y_format = ',.0f';
                    y_title = "数量"
                elif view_mode == "Order":
                    y_format = ',.0f';
                    y_title = "订单数"
                else:
                    y_format = ',.0f';
                    y_title = "数值"

                # 基础图表对象
                base = alt.Chart(df_chart_melt).encode(
                    x=alt.X('日期:T', title=None),
                    tooltip=['日期:T', '指标', alt.Tooltip('数值', format=y_format, title=y_title)]
                )

                # 图层1: 主折线 (圆滑)
                line_chart = base.mark_line(interpolate='monotone', strokeWidth=3).encode(
                    y=alt.Y('数值:Q', title=y_title, axis=alt.Axis(format=y_format)),
                    color=alt.Color('指标', legend=alt.Legend(orient='bottom', title=None))
                )

                # 条件: 仅选中 1 个项目时，显示辅助线
                if len(show_cols) == 1:
                    # 图层2: 趋势线 (Trendline) - 灰色虚线
                    # 使用 transform_calculate 注入 "趋势线" 标签以显示在图例中
                    trend_line = base.transform_regression(
                        '日期', '数值', method="linear"
                    ).transform_calculate(
                        Trend="'趋势线'"
                    ).mark_line(
                        strokeDash=[5, 5], color='gray', opacity=0.8
                    ).encode(
                        # 映射到一个常量颜色，为了让它出现在 Legend
                        color=alt.Color('Trend:N', legend=alt.Legend(orient='bottom', title=None),
                                        scale=alt.Scale(range=['gray']))
                    )

                    # 图层3: 平均线 (Average Rule) - 橙色虚线
                    # 使用 transform_joinaggregate 计算全局平均值
                    avg_line = base.transform_joinaggregate(
                        mean_val='mean(数值)'
                    ).transform_calculate(
                        Avg="'平均线'"
                    ).mark_rule(
                        strokeDash=[4, 2], color='#FFA500'
                    ).encode(
                        y='mean_val:Q',
                        color=alt.Color('Avg:N', legend=alt.Legend(orient='bottom', title=None),
                                        scale=alt.Scale(range=['#FFA500']))
                    )

                    final_chart = (line_chart + trend_line + avg_line).resolve_scale(color='independent')
                else:
                    final_chart = line_chart

                final_chart = final_chart.properties(
                    padding={'left': 60, 'right': 20, 'top': 10, 'bottom': 10}
                )
                st.altair_chart(final_chart, use_container_width=True)
            else:
                st.info(f"请勾选左侧筛选器以显示 {view_mode} 数据。")

            # [Removed] 原始数据框已彻底移除

    if not stores:
        st.toast("请选择店铺", icon="🚨")

==================== END FILE: ui/pages/data_visualization.py ====================


==================== START FILE: ui/pages/ai_gemini.py ====================
# ui/pages/ai_gemini.py

import os
import time
import streamlit as st
import google.generativeai as genai
import requests
import datetime
from config import Config
from core.context import get_current_user
from core.services.chat_service import ChatService
from ui.utils import get_client_ip  # [DRY Refactor] 引入公共工具


@st.cache_data(ttl=600)
def get_environment_context(ip: str) -> str:
    """获取环境上下文 (缓存)"""
    context_str = f"用户 IP: {ip}\n"
    if ip in ["UNKNOWN", "127.0.0.1", "localhost"]:
        return context_str + "位置: 本地开发环境 (未知位置)"
    try:
        loc_res = requests.get(f"http://ip-api.com/json/{ip}", timeout=2).json()
        if loc_res.get("status") == "success":
            city = loc_res.get("city", "Unknown")
            timezone = loc_res.get("timezone", "UTC")
            context_str += f"用户位置: {city} (时区: {timezone})\n"

            # 获取天气
            lat, lon = loc_res["lat"], loc_res["lon"]
            w_url = f"https://api.open-meteo.com/v1/forecast?latitude={lat}&longitude={lon}&current_weather=true&timezone={timezone}"
            w_res = requests.get(w_url, timeout=2).json()
            if "current_weather" in w_res:
                curr = w_res["current_weather"]
                context_str += f"当前天气: 气温 {curr['temperature']}°C\n"

            # 获取时间
            try:
                import pytz
                local_tz = pytz.timezone(timezone)
                now = datetime.datetime.now(local_tz).strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
                context_str += f"当地时间: {now}\n"
            except:
                pass
    except:
        pass
    return context_str


def render():
    # 1. 初始化服务
    user = get_current_user() or "anonymous"
    chat_service = ChatService(user)

    # 2. API Key 检查
    api_key = os.getenv("GOOGLE_API_KEY")
    if not api_key:
        st.error(" 未配置 GOOGLE_API_KEY。")
        return

    # 3. CSS 优化
    st.markdown("""
        <style>
        .chat-row {
            padding: 10px;
            border-radius: 5px;
            margin-bottom: 5px;
            background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.05);
            transition: background-color 0.3s;
            cursor: pointer;
        }
        .chat-row:hover {
            background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1);
        }
        .chat-active {
            background-color: rgba(78, 201, 176, 0.2) !important;
            border-left: 3px solid #4EC9B0;
        }
        </style>
    """, unsafe_allow_html=True)

    # 4. 布局：左侧历史，右侧对话
    col_sidebar, col_chat = st.columns([1, 3.5])

    # ===========================
    # 左侧：会话列表
    # ===========================
    with col_sidebar:
        if st.button("➕ 新建对话", use_container_width=True, type="primary"):
            chat_service.create_session()
            st.rerun()

        st.markdown("---")
        st.caption("🕒 历史记录")

        # 获取所有会话
        sessions = chat_service.get_all_sessions()
        active_info = chat_service.get_active_session()
        active_id = active_info["id"]

        # 渲染列表
        with st.container(height=600, border=False):
            for s in sessions:
                sid = s["id"]
                title = s["title"]
                is_active = (sid == active_id)

                # 使用列布局实现：标题 + 删除按钮
                c_text, c_del = st.columns([4, 1])

                # 标题按钮 (切换会话)
                btn_type = "secondary" if not is_active else "primary"
                if c_text.button(f"💬 {title}", key=f"sel_{sid}", help=s["updated_at"], use_container_width=True,
                                 type=btn_type):
                    chat_service.set_active_session(sid)
                    st.rerun()

                # 删除按钮
                if c_del.button("🗑️", key=f"del_{sid}", help="删除此会话"):
                    chat_service.delete_session(sid)
                    st.rerun()

    # ===========================
    # 右侧：聊天窗口
    # ===========================
    with col_chat:
        current_session = active_info["data"]

        # 标题栏
        st.markdown(f"### 🤖 {current_session.get('title', 'Google Gemini')}")
        st.caption("Powered by Gemini 2.0 Flash | 🔒 独立记忆空间")

        # 获取环境上下文 (懒加载)
        if "ai_context_str" not in st.session_state:
            # [Refactor] 调用公共 IP 函数
            ip = get_client_ip()
            st.session_state.ai_context_str = get_environment_context(ip)

        # 初始化模型
        try:
            genai.configure(api_key=api_key)
            system_instruction = f"""
            你是一个专业的企业 ERP 智能助手 (Eaglestar ERP Assistant)。
            【当前用户环境信息】
            {st.session_state.ai_context_str}
            【你的职责】
            1. 回答关于库存管理、供应链、数据分析的通用问题。
            2. 保持回答简洁、专业。
            """
            model = genai.GenerativeModel(model_name='gemini-2.0-flash', system_instruction=system_instruction)
        except Exception as e:
            st.error(f"模型连接失败: {e}")
            return

        # 渲染消息流
        messages = current_session.get("messages", [])
        for msg in messages:
            with st.chat_message(msg["role"]):
                st.markdown(msg["content"])

        # 处理输入
        if prompt := st.chat_input("请输入您的问题..."):
            # 1. 记录用户消息
            chat_service.add_message(active_id, "user", prompt)
            with st.chat_message("user"):
                st.markdown(prompt)

            # 2. 生成回复
            with st.chat_message("assistant"):
                message_placeholder = st.empty()
                full_response = ""
                try:
                    # 构造上下文 (Gemini 格式)
                    chat_history = []
                    for m in messages:
                        role = "user" if m["role"] == "user" else "model"
                        chat_history.append({"role": role, "parts": [m["content"]]})

                    chat = model.start_chat(history=chat_history)
                    response = chat.send_message(prompt, stream=True)

                    for chunk in response:
                        if chunk.text:
                            full_response += chunk.text
                            message_placeholder.markdown(full_response + "▌")

                    message_placeholder.markdown(full_response)

                    # 3. 记录助手回复
                    chat_service.add_message(active_id, "assistant", full_response)

                    # 如果是第一轮对话，刷新页面以更新左侧标题
                    if len(messages) == 0:
                        st.rerun()

                except Exception as e:
                    st.error(f"AI 响应异常: {e}")
==================== END FILE: ui/pages/ai_gemini.py ====================


==================== START FILE: tools/restore_project.py ====================
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
# tools/restore_project.py
"""
从 project_all_code_*.txt 恢复整个项目结构。
位置：tools/restore_project.py
"""

import sys
import re
from pathlib import Path

# 匹配 START/END 标记
START_PATTERN = re.compile(r"^=+\s*START (?:SPECIAL )?FILE:\s*(.+?)\s*=+\s*$")
END_PATTERN = re.compile(r"^=+\s*END FILE:\s*(.+?)\s*=+\s*$")


def parse_project_root_hint(line: str) -> Path | None:
    prefix = "Project Root:"
    if line.startswith(prefix):
        path_str = line[len(prefix):].strip()
        if path_str:
            return Path(path_str).expanduser()
    return None


def write_file(base_dir: Path, rel_path: str, content: str):
    target_path = base_dir / rel_path
    # 安全检查：防止写入到项目根目录之外
    try:
        target_path.resolve().relative_to(base_dir.resolve())
    except ValueError:
        print(f"⚠️ 跳过非法路径 (越界): {rel_path}")
        return

    target_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    with target_path.open("w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        f.write(content)


def restore_from_txt(txt_path: Path, base_dir: Path | None = None):
    if not txt_path.is_file():
        print(f" 找不到 TXT 文件: {txt_path}")
        sys.exit(1)

    print(f"📄 正在读取快照 TXT: {txt_path}")

    detected_root: Path | None = None
    current_file: str | None = None
    buffer: list[str] = []
    files_written = 0

    # 1. 扫描 Project Root
    with txt_path.open("r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        for line in f:
            if detected_root is None:
                detected_root = parse_project_root_hint(line)
            if detected_root is not None:
                break

    # 2. 确定 Base Dir
    if base_dir is None:
        if detected_root is not None:
            base_dir = detected_root
            print(f"📁 使用 TXT 记录的根目录: {base_dir}")
        else:
            # [Fix] 脚本在 tools/ 下，默认还原到项目根目录 (tools 的上一级)
            base_dir = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent
            print(f"⚠️ TXT 未记录 Root，默认还原到: {base_dir}")
    else:
        base_dir = base_dir.resolve()
        print(f"📁 使用指定根目录: {base_dir}")

    # 3. 解析并写入
    with txt_path.open("r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        for raw_line in f:
            line = raw_line.rstrip("\n")

            m_start = START_PATTERN.match(line.strip())
            if m_start:
                if current_file is not None:
                    # 强制写入上一个未闭合文件
                    write_file(base_dir, current_file, "".join(buffer))
                    files_written += 1

                current_file = m_start.group(1).strip()
                buffer = []
                print(f"🟢 恢复: {current_file}")
                continue

            m_end = END_PATTERN.match(line.strip())
            if m_end and current_file is not None:
                write_file(base_dir, current_file, "".join(buffer))
                files_written += 1
                current_file = None
                buffer = []
                continue

            if current_file is not None:
                buffer.append(raw_line)

    if current_file is not None and buffer:
        write_file(base_dir, current_file, "".join(buffer))
        files_written += 1

    print("=====================================")
    print(f"🎉 恢复完成，共写入 {files_written} 个文件")
    print(f"📦 项目位置: {base_dir}")


def auto_detect_txt_in_root() -> Path | None:
    """
    [Fix] 在项目根目录 (tools/..) 寻找 project_all_code_*.txt
    """
    project_root = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent
    # 优先找 VersionHistory 下的，或者根目录下的
    candidates = sorted(project_root.glob("project_all_code_*.txt"))
    if not candidates:
        # 再试着找 VersionHistory 文件夹
        vh_dir = project_root / "VersionHistory"
        if vh_dir.exists():
            candidates = sorted(vh_dir.glob("project_all_code_*.txt"))

    return candidates[-1] if candidates else None  # 取最新的


def main():
    if len(sys.argv) >= 2:
        txt_path = Path(sys.argv[1]).expanduser()
        base_dir = Path(sys.argv[2]).expanduser() if len(sys.argv) >= 3 else None
    else:
        txt_path = auto_detect_txt_in_root()
        base_dir = None
        if txt_path is None:
            print(" 未在项目根目录找到 project_all_code_*.txt")
            print("   用法: python tools/restore_project.py <path_to_txt> [target_dir]")
            sys.exit(1)
        print(f"🔍 自动检测到最新快照: {txt_path.name}")

    restore_from_txt(txt_path, base_dir)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
==================== END FILE: tools/restore_project.py ====================


==================== START FILE: tools/scan_old_refs.py ====================
# tools/scan_old_refs.py
import os

# 要查找的旧文件名
TARGET_STRING = "run_test_app.py"

# 忽略的目录 (保留 .vscode 和 .idea 以便检查 IDE 配置)
IGNORE_DIRS = {'.git', '.venv', '__pycache__', 'logs', 'backup', 'VersionHistory'}


def scan_project():
    # 获取项目根目录 (tools 的上一级)
    project_root = os.path.dirname(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)))
    print(f"🔍 正在扫描项目根目录: {project_root}")
    print(f"🎯 寻找残留引用: '{TARGET_STRING}'\n")

    found_count = 0

    for root, dirs, files in os.walk(project_root):
        # 过滤忽略的目录
        dirs[:] = [d for d in dirs if d not in IGNORE_DIRS]

        for file in files:
            # 跳过脚本自己
            if file == "scan_old_refs.py": continue

            file_path = os.path.join(root, file)

            try:
                with open(file_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8', errors='ignore') as f:
                    content = f.read()
                    if TARGET_STRING in content:
                        print(f"🚨 发现残留! -> {os.path.relpath(file_path, project_root)}")
                        # 打印具体行内容
                        f.seek(0)
                        for i, line in enumerate(f):
                            if TARGET_STRING in line:
                                print(f"   Line {i + 1}: {line.strip()}")
                        print("-" * 40)
                        found_count += 1
            except Exception as e:
                # 跳过二进制文件或无法读取的文件
                pass

    if found_count == 0:
        print(" 恭喜！项目中未发现任何旧文件名引用。")
        print("👉 如果依然报错，请检查 IDE (PyCharm/VSCode) 的 'Run Configuration' 设置。")
    else:
        print(f" 共发现 {found_count} 处残留，请手动修改。")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    scan_project()
==================== END FILE: tools/scan_old_refs.py ====================

# tools/check_models.py
import os

    try:
        count = 0
        for m in genai.list_models():

                print(f" 模型名称: {m.name}")
                print(f"   描述: {m.description}")
                print("-" * 40)
                count += 1

        if count == 0:
            print("⚠️ 未找到支持 generateContent 的模型。")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f" 查询失败: {e}")
